seehttpgretilsubunigoettingendegretilhtmNamo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā sambuddhassaMahānipāto Mugapakkhajātakaṃ  Mā paṇḍitiyaṃ vibhāvaya bālamato bhava sabbapāṇinaṃSabbo jano taṃ ocināyatu evaṃ tava attho bhavissati Karomi te taṃ vacanaṃ yaṃ maṃ bhaṇasi devateAtthakāmāsi me amma hitakāmāsi devate  Kinnusantaramānova kāsuṃ khaṇasi sārathiPuṭṭho me samma akkhāhi kiṃ kāsuyā karissasi Rañño mugo ca pakkho ca putto jāto acetasoSombhi raññā samajjhiṭṭho puttaṃ me nikhaṇaṃ vane Na khadhiro na mugosmi na pakkho napi paṅguloAdhammaṃ sārathi kayirā mañce tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane  Ūrū bāhu ca me passa bhāsitañca suṇohi meAdhammaṃ sārathi kayirā mañce tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane Devatānusi gandhabbo ādu sakko purindadoKo vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ Nambhi devo na gandhabbo napi sakko purindadoKāsirañño ahaṃ putto yaṃ kāsuyā nighaññasi Paṇḍiccayaṃ  machasaṃ syā vi  Tañajato  machasaṃ syā Samajjhattho  machasaṃ syā  Nikkhaṇaṃ  machasaṃ syā Vikalo  syā piṅgalo  machasaṃ  Adu  machasaṃ  Nāpi nambhi  machasaṃ syā  Tassa rañño ahaṃ putto yaṃ tvaṃ samupajivasi Adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā maṃ ve tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vāNa tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubho hi pāpako Yathā rukkho rājā yathā sākhā tathā ahaṃYathā chāyupago poso evaṃ tvamasi sārathiAdhammaṃ sārathi kayirā maṃ ve tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane  Pahutabhakkho bhavanti vippavuttho sakāgharā Bahu naṃ upajivanti yo mittānaṃ na dubhati Yaṃ yaṃ janapadaṃ yāti nigame rājadhāniyo Sabbattha pujito hoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati Nāssa corā pasahanti nātimaññeti khattiyoSabbe amitte tarati yo mittānaṃ na dubhati Akkuddho sagharaṃ eti sabhāya paṭinanditoÑātinaṃ uttamo hoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati Sakkatvā sakkato hoti garu hoti sagāravo Vaṇṇakittibhato hoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati Pujako labhate pujaṃ vandako paṭivandataṃYaso kittiñca pappoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati Aggi yathā pajjalati devatāva virocatiSiriyā ajahito hoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati Sammupajivasi  machasaṃ  Mitatadubbho  machasaṃ vi  Nikkhaṇaṃ  machasaṃ Bahutta  machasaṃ  Vipapamutto   Sakaṅgharā  machasaṃ sya  Na dubbhati machasaṃ  Rājaṭṭhāniyo  machasaṃ  Nātimaññati  machasaṃ Akuḍo  machasaṃ  Sahāyaṃ  machasaṃ  Garuko hoti gāravo  machasaṃ  Gāvo tassa pajāyanti khette vuttaṃ virūhatiVuttānaṃ phalamasanāti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati Darito pabbatāno vā rukkhāto patito naroCuto patiṭṭhaṃ labhati yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati Virūḷhamulasantānaṃ nigrodhamiva mālutoAmittā nappasahanti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  Ehi taṃ paṭinessāmi rājaputta sakaṃ gharaṃRajjaṃ kārehi bhaddante kiṃ araññe karissasi Alaṃ me tena rajjena ñātakehi dhanena vāYaṃ me adhammacariyāya rajjaṃ labbhetha sārathi Puṇṇapattaṃ palabbhehi rājaputta ito gatoPitā mātā ca me dajjuṃ rājaputta tayī gate Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāTepi attamanā dajjuṃ rājaputta tayī gate Hatthārūhā aṇikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakāTepi dajjuṃ patitā me rājaputta tayī gate Bahu jānapadā caññe negamā ca samāgatā upāyanāni me dajjuṃ rājaputta tayī gate  Pitumātu cahaṃ catto raṭṭhassa nigamassa caAtho sakyakumārānaṃ natthi mayhaṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ Anuññāto ahaṃ matyā sañcatto pitarā ahaṃEko araññe pabbajito na kāme abhipatthaye Api ataramānānaṃ phalāsāva samijjhatiVipakkabrahmacariyosmi evaṃ jānāhi sārathi Vutatāna phala  machasaṃ  Pabbato  machasaṃ  Rukkhato  machasaṃ Ñātakena  machasaṃ syā  Labhetha  machasaṃ  Maṃ palābhehi  syā maṃ lābhehi Rohā  machasaṃ vi  Bahuttadhaññā  machasaṃ syā  Api ataramānānaṃ sammadatthā vipaccatiVipakkabrahmacariyosmi nikkhanto akutobhayo Evaṃ vaggukatho santo vissaṭṭhaccano casi  kasmāpitucca mātucca santike nabhaṇi tadā Nāhaṃ asanthitā pakkho na badhiro asotatāNāhaṃ ajivhatā mugo mā maṃ mugamadhārayi Purimaṃ sarāmahaṃ jātiṃ yattha rajjamakārayiṃKārayitvā tahiṃ rajjaṃ pāpatthaṃ nirayaṃ bhusaṃ Visatiñceva vassāni tahiṃ rajjamakārayiṃAsitivassasahassāni nirayamhi apaccisaṃ  Tassa rajjassahaṃ bhīto mā maṃ rajjābhisecayuṃTasmā pitucca mātucca santike na bhaṇiṃ tadā Ucchaṅge maṃ nisīdetvā pitā atthānusāsatiEkaṃ hanatha bandhatha ekaṃ khārāpatacchikaṃEkaṃ sulasmiṃ appetha iccassamanusāsati Tassāhaṃ pharusaṃ sutvā vācāyo samudiritāAmugo mugavaṇṇena apakkho pakkhasammatoSake muttakarisasmiṃ acchāhaṃ samparipaluto Kasirañca parittañca tañca dukkhena saṃyutaṃKo taṃ jīvitamāgamma veraṃ kayirātha kenaci Paññāya ca alābhena dhammassa ca adassanāKo taṃ jīvitamāgamma veraṃ kayirātha kenaci Api ataramānānaṃ phalāsāva samijjhatiVipakkabrahmacariyosmi evaṃ jānāhi sārathi Vaggukato  machasaṃ  Vacanova so  machasaṃ syā  Tasmā  vi Asandhitā  machasaṃ syā  Asandhitā  machasaṃ syā  Apaccasaṃ  syā apaccayiṃ vi  Pituva mātuva  machasaṃ syā  Kharā  machasaṃ syā Uppetha  machasaṃ uppetha  syā  Tāsāhaṃ  machasaṃ tyāhaṃ  syā accetha  vi Apakkhe  machasaṃ  Api ataramānānaṃ sammadattho vipaccatiVipakkabrahmacariyosmi nikkhanto akutobhayo  Ahmapi pabbajissāmi rājaputta tavantikeAvhayassu maṃ bhaddaneta pabbajjā mama ruccati Rathaṃ niyyādayitvāna anaṇo ehi sārathiAnaṇassa hi pabbajjā etaṃ isihi vaṇṇitaṃ Yadeva tyāhaṃ vacanaṃ akaraṃ bhaddamatthu teTadeva me tvaṃ vacanaṃ yācito kattumarahasi Idheva tāva acchassu yāva rājānamānayeAppeva te pitā disvā pitato sumano siyā  Karomi te taṃ vacanaṃ yaṃ maṃ bhaṇasi sārathiAhmapi daṭṭhukāmosmi pitaraṃ me idhāgataṃ Ehi samma nivattassu kusalaṃ vajjāsi ñātinaṃMātaraṃ pitaraṃ mayhaṃ vutto vajjāsi vandanaṃ Tassa pāde gahetvāna katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃSārathi rathamāruyha rājadvāraṃ upāgami Suññaṃ mātā rathaṃ disvā ekaṃ sārathimāgataṃAssupuṇṇehi nettehi rodanti naṃ udikkhati Aya so sārathi eti nihanatvāna mamatujaṃNihato nūna me putto pathavyā bhumivaddhano Amittā nūna nandanti patitā nūna verinoĀgataṃ sārathiṃ disvā nihanatvāna mamatujaṃ Suññaṃ mātā rathaṃ disvā ekaṃ sārathimāgataṃAssupuṇṇehi nettehi rodanti paripucchati Nihanatvā mama atrajaṃ  machasaṃ  Rodanti naṃ paripucchi  machasaṃ  Kinnu mugo kinnu pakkho kinnu so vilapi tadāNihaññamāno bhumiyā taṃ me akkhāhi sārathi Kathaṃ hatthehi pādehi mugo pakkho vivajjayiNihaññamāno bhumiyā taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito  Akkhissaṃ te ahaṃ ayye dajjāsi abhayaṃ mamaYaṃ me sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā rājaputtassa santike Abhayaṃ samma te dammi abhito bhaṇa sārathiYaṃ te sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā rājaputtassa santike Na so mugo na so pakko vissaṭṭhavacanova soRajjassa kira so bhito akari ālaye bahu Purimaṃ sarati so jātiṃ yattha rajjamakārayiKārayitvā tahiṃ rajjaṃ pāpattha nirayaṃ bhusaṃ Visatiñce ca vassāni tahiṃ rajjamakārayiAsiti vassa sahassāni nirayamhi apacci so Tassa rājassa so bhīto mā maṃ rajjābhisecayuṃ Tasmā pitucca mātucca santike na bhaṇi tadā Aṅgapaccaṅga sampanno ārohapariṇābhavāVissaṭṭhava vano pañño magge saggassa tiṭṭhati Sace tvaṃ daṭṭhukāmāsi rājaputti tavatrajaṃEhi taṃ pāpayissāmi yattha sammati temiyo  Yojayantu rathe asse kacchaṃ nāgāna bandhathaUdirayantu saṅkhapaṇavā vadantu ekapokkharā Nadantu bheri sannaddhā vagguṃ vadatu dundubhīNegamā ca maṃ anventu gacchaṃ puttanivedako Akkheyyante  machasaṃ syā  Visaṭṭha  machasaṃ Akarā  machasaṃ syā  Apaccisa  machasaṃ Rajjebhisecayuṃ  machasaṃ  Pituca mātuva Nabhaṇe  machasaṃ  Kāmosi  machasaṃ Rājaputtaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Nāgāni  machasaṃ syā Vagguvādantu  machasaṃ  Nivādako  machasaṃ  Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāKhippaṃ yānāni yojentu gacchaṃ puttanivedako Hatthārohā aṇikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārākāKhippaṃ yānāni yojentu gacchaṃ puttanivedako Samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatāKhippaṃ yānāni yojentu gacchaṃ puttanivedako  Asse ca sārathi yutte sindhave sīghavāhaneRājadvāraṃ upāgañachuṃ yuttā deva ime bhayā Thulā javena bhāyanti kisā bhāyanti thāmunā Kise thule vivajjetvā saṃsaṭṭhā yojitā bhayā Tato rājā taramāno yuttamāruyha sandanaṃItthāgāraṃ ajjhabhāsi sabbāva anuyātha maṃ Vāḷavijanimuṇibhisaṃ khaggaṃ chattaṃ ca paṇḍaraṃUpādirathamāruyha suvaṇṇena alaṅkato Tato ca rājā pāyāsi purakkhatvāna sārathiKhippameva upāgañachi yattha sammati temiyo  Tañca disvāna āyantaṃ jalantamiva tejasāKhattasaṅghaparibbuḷhaṃ temiyo etadabravi Kaccinnu tāta kusalaṃ kacci tāta anāmayaṃKacacinnu rājakaññāyo arogā mayha mātaro Kusalañceva me putta atho putta anāmayaṃSabbāva rājakaññāyo arogā tuyha mātaro Kaccissa majjapo tāta kacci te suramappiyaṃKacci sacce ca dhamme ca dāne te ramati mano Thāmasā  syā kāmunā  machasaṃ  Abhāsatha  machasaṃ ajjhabhāsittha  vi Suvaṇṇehi  machasaṃ  Alaṅkatā  machasaṃ syā Purakkhitvāna  machasaṃ syā  Paribuḷhaṃ  machasaṃ Kaccinu  machasaṃ  Sabbā ca  machasaṃ  Kacci amajjapo  machasaṃ syā  Amajjapo ahaṃ puttaṃ atho me suramappiyaṃAtho sacce ca dhamme ca dāne me ramati mano Kacci arogaṃ yoggaṃ te kacci vahati vāhanaṃKacci te vyādhayo natthi sarirassupatāpanā Atho arogaṃ yoggaṃ me ato vahati vāhanaṃAtho me vyādhayo natthi sarirassupatāpanā Kacci antā ca te phitā majjhe ca bahalā tavaKoṭṭhāgārañca kosaññaca kacci te paṭisanthataṃ  Atho antā ca te phitā majjhe ca bahalā mamaKoṭṭhāgārañca kosaññaca sabbaṃ me paṭisanthataṃ Svāgataṃ te mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃPatiṭāpentu pallaṅkaṃ pattha rājā nisakkati  Idheva te nisinnassa niyate paṇṇasanthate Etto udakamādāya pāde pakkhālayantu te Idampi paṇṇakaṃ mayhaṃ randhaṃ rāja aloṇakaṃMaṃ lābhehi  Rohā  machasaṃ vi  Bahuttadhaññā  machasaṃ syā Na cāhaṃ paṇṇaṃ bhuñjāmi na hetaṃ mayha bhojanaṃSālinaṃ odanaṃ bhuñeja suciṃ maṃsupasevanaṃ Accherakaṃ maṃ paṭibhāti ekakampi rabhogataṃEdisaṃ bhuñjamānānaṃ kena vaṇṇo pasidati  Eko rāja nipajjāmi niyate paṇṇasanthateTāya me ekaseyyāya rāja vaṇṇo pasidati Na ce nettiṃsabaddhā me rājarakkhā upaṭṭhitāTāya me sukhāseyyāya rāja vaṇṇo pasidati Vāhati  machasaṃ syā vi  Tāpiyā  machasaṃ syā Sandhataṃ  machasaṃ  Santhare  machasaṃ Navāhaṃ  machasaṃ  Suci  machasaṃ syā  Nava  machasaṃ  Atitaṃ nānusocāmi nappajappamanāgataṃPaccuppannena yāpemi tena vaṇṇo pasidati Anāgatappajappāya atitassasocanāEtena bālā sussanti naḷova bharito luto Hatthāṇikaṃ rathāṇikaṃ asse patti ca vamminoNivesanāni rammāni ahaṃ putta dadāmi te Itthāgārampi te dammi sabbālaṅkarā bhusitaṃTā putta paṭipajjassu tvaṃ no rājā bhavissasi Kusalā naccagitassa sikkhitā caturitthiyoKame taṃ ramayissanti kiṃ araññe karissasi Paṭirājuhi te kaññā ānayissaṃ alaṅkatāTāsu putte janetvāna atha pacchā pabbajissasi Yuvā ca daharo cāsi paṭhamuppattite susuRajjaṃ kārehi bhaddante kiṃ araññe karissasi Yuvā care buhmacariyaṃ brahmacāri yuvā siyāDaharassa hi pabbajjā etaṃ isihi vaṇṇitaṃ  Yuvā care buhmacariyaṃ brahmacāri yuvā siyāBrahmacariyaṃ carissāmi nāhaṃ rajjenamatthiko Passāmi vohaṃ daharaṃ amma tāta vadaṃ naraṃ Kicchā laddhaṃ piyaṃ puttaṃ apapatvāna jaraṃ mataṃ Passāmi vohaṃ dahariṃ kumāriṃ cāru dassanaṃNaḷavaṃsakaḷiraṃva paluggaṃ jīvitakkhaye Vadantaraṃ  machasaṃ syā vi  Daharāpi hi miyanti narā ca atha nāriyoTattha ko vissase poso daharomhīti jivite Yasasa ratyā vivasane āyuṃ appataraṃ siyāAppodakeva macchānaṃ kinnu komārakaṃ tahiṃ Niccamabbhāhato loko niccañca parivāritoAmoghāsu vajantisu kiṃ maṃ rajjena siñcasi Kenamabbhāhato loko kena ca parivāritoKāyo amoghā gacchanti taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito Maccunābbhāhato loko jarāya parivāritoRatyo amoghā gacchanti evaṃ jānāhi khattiya Yathāpi tante vitate yaṃ yadevupavīyayatiAppakaṃ hoti vetabbaṃ evaṃ maccāna jīvitaṃ Yathā vārivaho puro gacchannupanivatti Evamāyu manussānaṃ gacchannupanivattati Yathā vārivaho puro vahe rukkhupakulaje Evaṃ jarāya maraṇena vuyhante vata pāṇino   Hatthāṇikaṃ rathāṇikaṃ asse patti ca vamminoNivesanāni rammani ahaṃ puttadadāmi te Itthāgārampi te dammi sabbālaṅkārabhusitaṃTā putta paṭipajjassu tvaṃ no rājā bhavissasi Kusalā naccagītassa sikkhitā caturitthiyoKāme taṃ ramayissanti kiṃ araññe karissasi Vitante  machasaṃ syā  Gacchaṃ nuparivattati  machasaṃ gacchaṃ na parivattati  syā Ruhepakulaje  Sabbapāṇino  machasaṃ syā  Paṭipuhi te kaññā ānayissaṃ ajaṅkatāTāsu putte janetvāna atha pacchā pabbajissasi Yuvā ca daharo cāsi paṭhamuppattito susuRajjaṃ karehi bhaddante kiṃ araññe karissasi Koṭṭhāgārañca kosañca vāhanāni balāni caNivesanāni rammāni ahaṃ punta dadāmi te Gomaṇḍalaparibbuḷho dāsisaṅghapurakkhatoRajjaṃ kārehi bhaddanne kiṃ araññe karissasi Kiṃ dhanena yaṃ jiyetha kiṃ bhariyāyaya marissatiKiṃ yobbanena ciṇṇena yaṃ jarā abhihessati  Tattha kā vandi kā khiḍḍā kā ratī kā dhanesanā Ki me puttehi dārehi rāja muttosmi bandhanā Sohaṃ evaṃ pajānāmi maccu me nappamajjatiAntakenādhipantassa kā rati kā dhanesanā  Phalānamiva pakkānaṃ niccaṃ patanato bhayaṃEvaṃ jātānamaccānaṃ niccaṃ maraṇato bhayaṃ Sāyameke na dissanti pato diṭṭhā bahujjanāPato eke na dissanti sāyaṃ diṭṭhā bahujjanā Ajjeva kiccaṃ ātappaṃ ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suveNahi no saṅgaraṃ tena mahāsenena maccunā Corā dhanassa patthessa rājā muttosmi bandhanāEhi rāja nivattassu nāhaṃ rajjenamatthikotiMugapakkhajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ Yaṃ jarāyābhibhuyyati  machasaṃ syā  Dhanesinā  machasaṃ syā Passanti  vi  Ātapa  machasaṃ  Mahājanakajātakaṃ  Koyaṃ majjhe samudadasmiṃ apassaṃ tiramāyuheKaṃ tvaṃ atthavasaṃ ñatvā evaṃ vāyamase bhusaṃ Nisamma vattaṃ lokassa vāyāmassa ca devateTasmā majjhe samuddasmiṃ appasaṃ tiramāyuhe Gambhīre appameyyasmiṃ tīraṃ yassa na dissatiMogho te purisa vāyāmo appatvāva marissi  Anaṇo ñātinaṃ hoti devānaṃ pituno ca soKaraṃ purisakiccāni na ca pacchānutappati Apāraneyyaṃ yaṃ kammaṃ aphalaṃ kilamathuddayaṃTattha ko vāyamenattho maccu yassābhinippataṃ  Apāraneyyaṃ accantaṃ yo viditvāna devateNa rakkhe attano pāṇaṃ jaññā so yadi hāpaye Adhippāya phalaṃ eke asmiṃ lokasmi devatePayojayanti kammāni tāni ijjhanti vā na vā Sandiṭṭhikaṃ kammaphalaṃ nanu passasi devateSannā aññe tarāmahaṃ tañca passāmi santike So ahaṃ vāyamissāmi yathāsattiṃ yathābalaṃGacchaṃ pāraṃ samuddassa kāsaṃ purisakāriyaṃ  Yo tvaṃ evaṃ gate oghe appameyye mahaṇṇaveDhammavāyāmasampanno kammanā nāvasidasiSo tvaṃ tattheva gacchābhi yattha te nirato mano Kiṃ  machasaṃ Syā  Pitunañca  machasaṃ syā  Nipaphataṃ  syā Yati  machasaṃ  Kassaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Kammunā  machasaṃ syā Ke  machasaṃ  Suriyuggamane nidhi atho oggamane nidhiAnno nidhi bahi nidhi na anto na bahi nidhi  Ārohane mahānidhi atho orohane nidhiCaturo ca mahāsālā samantā yojane nidhi Dantaggesu mahānidhi vālaggesu ca kekhukeRukkhaggesu mahānidi soḷasete mahānidhiSahassatthāmo pallaṅko sivalārādhanena ca niccaṃ nigaḷa maṇḍitaKasmā te eko bhujo janati eko te na janati bhujo Imasmiṃ me samaṇa hatthe paṭimukko ekanīdhuro Saṅghātā jāyate saddo dutiyasseva sā gati Imasmiṃ me samaṇā hatthe paṭimukko ekanīdhuro So aditiyo na chanati munibhutova tiṭṭhati Vivādappatto dutiyo keneko vivadissatiTassa te saggakāmassa ekattamuparovataṃ  Suṇasi sivalī gāthā kumāriyā paveditāPessiyā maṃ garahittho dutiyasseva sā gati Ayaṃ dvedhā patho bhadde anuciṇṇo pathāvihiTesaṃ tvaṃ ekaṃ gaṇhāhi abhamekaṃ punāparaṃ Neva maṃ tvaṃ patī meti māhaṃ bhariyāti vā punaImameva kathaṃ kathayantā thuṇaṃ nagarupāgamuṃ machasaṃ   Sāmajātakaṃ Ko nu maṃ usunā vijjhi pattaṃ udahārakaṃ Khattiyo brāhmano vesso ko maṃ viddhā niliyasi  Na me maṃsāni khajjāni cammenattho na vijjatiAtha kena nu vaṇṇena viddheyyaṃ maṃ amaññatha Ko vā tvaṃ kasasa vā putte kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃPuṭṭho me samma akkhāhi kiṃ maṃ viddhā nilīyasi Rājāhamasmi kāsinaṃ piliyakkhoti maṃ viduLobhā raṭṭhaṃ pahatvāna migamesaṃ carāmahaṃ maṃ ñātayoĀmantayiṃsu jivantaṃ svājjevāhaṃ gato saye Viddhosmi puthusallena savisena yathā migoSakamhi lohite rāja passa semi paripluto Paṭicammagato sallaṃ passa vihāmi lohitaṃĀturo tyānu pucchāmi nimiDevatānusi gandhabbo ādu sakko purindado Na ca me tādiso vaṇṇo diṭṭho vā yadi vā sutoĀcikkha me tvaṃ bhaddante kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ Sa lomahaṭṭhaṃ ñatvāna vāsavo avacā nimiṃSakkohamasmi devindo āgatosmi tavantiko Alomahaṭṭho manujinda puccha pañhaṃ yadicchasiSo ca tena kātokāso vāsavaṃ avacā nimi Pucachāmi taṃ mahābāhu sabbabhūtānamissaraDānaṃ vā brahmacariyaṃ vākatamaṃsu mahapphalaṃ So puṭṭho naradevena vāsavo avacā nimiṃVipākaṃ brahmacariyassa jānaṃ akkhāsajānato Hītena brahmacariyena khattiye upapajjatiMajjhimena ca devantaṃ uttamena visujjhati Nahete pulabhā kāyā yāvayogena Vehāsayāme bahukā jātarūpassa nimmitāDaddallamānā ābhenti vijjuvabbhaghanantare Sitibhutesu  machasaṃ  Susamāhitaṃ  machasaṃ  Vitati hi maṃ vindati disvā pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathiIme nu macco kimakaṃsu sādhuṃYo modare saggapatto vimāne Tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathiVipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato Saddhāya suniviṭṭhāya saddhamme suppavediteAkaṃsu santhuvacanaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsanaṃ Tesaṃ etāni ṭhānāni yāni tvaṃ rāja passasi Viditāni te mahārāja āvāsaṃ pāpakamminaṃAtho kalyāṇakammānaṃ ṭhānāni vidatāni teUyyābhidāni rājisi devarājassa santikeVimānakaṇḍaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  Sahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ dibbaṃ yānaṃ adhiṭṭhitoYāyamāno mahārājā addā sīdantare nageDisvānāmantiyī sutaṃ ime ke nāma pabbatā Sudassano karavīko īsadharo yugandharoNemindharo vinatako assakaṇṇo giribrahā Ete sidantare nagā anupubbasamuggatāMahārājānamāvāsā yāni tvaṃ rāja passasi Anekarūpaṃ ruviraṃ nānāvitraṃ pakāsatiĀkiṇaṇaṃ indisehi vyaggheheva surakkhitaṃ  Vitati hi maṃ vindati disvā pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathiImaṃ nu dvāraṃ kimbhiññamāhuMānoramaṃ dissati duratova  Sāsane  machasaṃ  Purakkhitā  machasaṃ  Ayaṃ pāṭho syāmapotthake yeva dissati  Tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathiVipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato Cintakūṭoti yaṃ āhu devarājapavesanaṃSudassanassa girino dvāraṃ hetaṃ pakāsati Anekarūpaṃ ruciraṃ nānācitraṃ pakāsatiĀkiṇṇaṃ indisadisehi vyaggheve surakkhitaṃPavisetena rājisi arajaṃ bhumimakkama Sahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ dibbaṃ yānaṃ adhiṭṭhitoYāyamāno mahārājā addā devasabhaṃ idaṃ Yathā sarade ākāso nīlova patidissatiTathupamaṃ idaṃ vyambhaṃ veḷuriyāsu nimmitaṃ Vitati hi maṃ vindati disvā pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathiImaṃ nu vyambhaṃ kimabhiññamāhu Tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathiVipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato  Sudhammaṃ iti yamāhu passesā dissate sabhāVeḷuriyā rucirā citrā dhārayanti sunimmitā Aṭṭhaṃsā sukatā thambhā sabbe veḷuriyāmayāYattha devā tāvatiṃsā sabbe indapurohitā Atthaṃ devamanussānaṃ cintayantā samaccharePavisetena rājisi devānaṃ anumodanaṃ Taṃ devā paṭinandiṃsu disvā rājānamāgataṃSvāgataṃ te mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃ Nisidadāni rājisi devarājassa santikeSakkopi paṭinandittha vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ  Nimantayi ca kāmehi āsanena ca vāsavo sādhu khosi anuppatto āvāsaṃvasavantinaṃ Vasa devesu rājisi sabbakāmasamiddhisuTāvatiṃsesu devesu bhuñja kāme amānuse Yathā yācitakaṃ yānaṃ yathā yācitakaṃ dhanaṃEvaṃ sammapadamevetaṃ yaṃ parato dānapaccayā  Nacāhametaṃ icchāmi yaṃ parato dānapaccayāSayaṃ katāni puññāni taṃ me āveṇiyaṃ dhanaṃ Sohaṃ gantvā samussesu kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃDānena samacariyāya saṃyamena damena caYaṃ katvā sukhito hoti na ca pacchānutappati Bahupakāro no bhavaṃ mātalī devasārathiYo me kalyāṇakammānaṃ pāpāni paṭidassayi  Idaṃ vatvā nimirājā vedeho mithilaggabhoPuthuyaññaṃ yajitvāna saññamaṃ ajjhupāgamītiNimijātakaṃ catutthaṃ Nimantayittha  machasaṃ  Pāpānaṃ pacidassayi  machasaṃ  Khaṇḍahālajātakaṃ  Rājāsi luddakammo ekarājāti pupphavatiyā So vajanti sugatiṃ narā puññāni katvāna Kiṃ pana taṃ atidānaṃ ke ca avajjhā imasmiṃ lokasmiṃEtañca kho no akkhāhi yajissāma dadāma dānāni  Puttehi deva yajitabbaṃ mahesīhi negamehi ca usabhehiĀjāniyehi sunandañcaLakkhaṇavarūpapannā pasurā kira hotha yaññatthāya  Gahapatayopi vadetha puṇaṇamukhaṃ bhaddiyaṃ sigālañcaVaḍḍhañcāpi gahapatiṃ pasurā kira hotha yaññatthāya Luddakapposi  machasaṃ bhātupariyesanaṃ caraṃ Pabbate giriduggesu gāmesu nigamesu caOrena dasarattassa passa āgataṃ  Hatthā pamutto urago pāde te nipatī bhusaṃKacci taṃ nu ḍasī tāta mā bhāyi sukhito bhava  Neva mayhaṃ ayaṃ nāgo alaṃ dukkhāya kāyaciYāvatatthi abhiggāhā mayā bhiyyo na vijjati Konu brāhmaṇa vaṇeṇana datto parisamāgamāAvhayantu suyuddhena suṇātu parisā mamaṃ Saṃpamadditā  machasaṃ  Tesaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Subhogova machasaṃ syā Padhāciṃsu  machasaṃ syā  Pariṇāmatā  machasaṃ syā Bhissāmi  machasaṃ syā  Ratatarattassa  machasaṃ syā  Kacacitaṃ ḍaṃsito machasaṃ kaccisiṃnuḍato  syā  Tava  machasaṃ  Tvaṃ maṃ nāgena ālamba ahaṃ maṇḍukachāpiyāHotu no abbhutaṃ tattha āsahassehi pacañahi Ahaṃ hi vasumā aḍḍho tvaṃ daḷiddosi māṇava ko nu te paṭihogatthi upajutañcakiṃ siyā Upajutañca me assa pāṭibhogo ca tādisoHotu no abbhutaṃ tattha āsahassehi pañcahi  Suṇohi me mahārāja vacanaṃ bhaddamatthu tePañcantaṃ me sahasasānaṃ pāṭibhogohi kintimā Pettikaṃ vā iṇaṃ hoti yaṃ vā hoti sayaṃ kataṃKiṃ tvaṃ evaṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ dhanaṃ yācasi brāhmaṇa Ālambāno hi nāgena mamaṃ abhijigiṃsati Ahaṃ maṇḍukachāpiyā ḍaṃsasissāmi brāhmaṇaṃ Taṃ tvaṃ daṭṭhuṃ mahārāja ajja raṭṭhābhivaddhanaKhantasaṅghaparibbuḷho niyyāhi ahidassanaṃ Neva taṃ atimaññāmi sippavādena māṇavaAtimantosi sippena uragaṃ nāpacāyasi  Mayampi nātimaññama sippavādena brāhmaṇaṃAvisena ca nāgena bhusaṃ vañcayase janaṃ Evaṃ cetaṃ jano jaññā yathā jānāmi taṃ ahaṃNa tvaṃ lahasi ālamba sattumuṭṭhiṃ kuto dhanaṃ Kharājino jaṭi rummi datto parisamāgatoSo tvaṃ evaṃ gataṃ nāgaṃ aviso atimaññasi Opajutañca  machasaṃ  Assuto  machasaṃ assano  vi Ālambāyano ca syā alambano ca  Abijigisati  machasaṃ Lahesi  machasaṃ  Bhusamuṭṭhiṃ  machasaṃ syā  Dummi  machasaṃ Dittā  machasaṃ  Āsajja kho taṃ jaññāsi puṇaṇaṃ uggassa tejasāMaññe taṃ bhasmarāsivaṃ khippasā kairissati Siyā visaṃ siḷuttassa deḍḍhuhassa silābhunoNeva lohitasisassa visaṃ nāgassa vijjati Sutaṃ metaṃ arabhataṃ saññatānaṃ tapassinaṃIdha dānāni datvāna saggaṃ gacchanti dāyakāJivanto dehi dānāni yadi te atthi dātave Ayaṃ nāgo mahiddhiko tejasī duratikkamoTena taṃ ḍaṃsayissāmi so taṃ bhasmaṃ karissati Mayāpetaṃ sutaṃ samma saññatānaṃ tapassinaṃIdha dānini datvāna saggaṃ gacchanti dāyakāTvameva dehi jivanto yadi te atthi dāteve  Ayaṃ accimukhi nāma puṇṇā uggassa tejasāTena taṃ ḍaṃsayissāmi so taṃ bhasmaṃ karissati Yā dhītā dhataraṭṭhassa vemātā bhagini mamaSā dissatu accimukhi puṇaṇā uggassa tejasā Chamāyaṃ ce nisiñcissaṃ brahmadanta vijānahiTiṇalatāni osadhyo usasusseyyuṃ asaṃsayaṃ Addhaṃ ce pātayissāmi brahmadanta vijānahiSattavassānayaṃ devo na vasse na himaṃ pate  Udakañce nisiñcissaṃ brahmadanta vijānahiYāvatā odakā pāṇā mareyyuṃ macchakacchapāNagarappavesanakaṇḍaṃ niṭṭitaṃ Naṃ  machasaṃ  Tejaso  machasaṃ  Ajamukhi  machasaṃ Taṃḍaṃsatvājamukhi  machasaṃ ḍaṃsatu  syā  Udake ce  machasaṃ Yāvanetā  machasaṃ   Lokyaṃ sajantaṃ udakaṃ payāgasmiṃ patiṭṭhitaṃKo maṃ ajjhohari bhuto ogāḷhaṃ yamunaṃ nadiṃ Yadesalokādhipati yasassīBārāṇasimpakirahari samantatoTassāhaṃ putto uragusabhassaSubhagoti maṃ brāhmaṇa vedayanti Sace hi putto uragusabhassaKaṃsassa rañño amarādhipassaMahesakkho aññataro pitā teMaccesu mātā pana te atulyāNa tādiso arahati brāhmaṇassaDāsampi ohārituṃ mahānubhāvo  Rukkhaṃ nissāya vijjhittho phaṇeyyaṃ pātumāgataṃSo viddho duramasarā saravegena sekhavā  Taṃ tvaṃ patitamaddakkhi araññasmiṃ brahmaneSa maṃsakājamādāya sāyaṃ nigrodhupāgami Suvalāsiya saṅghuṭṭhaṃ piṃgiyaṃ santhatāyutaṃKokilābhirudaṃ rammaṃ dhuvaṃ haritasaddalaṃ Tattha te so pāturahu iddhiyā yasasā jalaṃMahānubhāvo bhātā me kaññāhi parivārito So tena pariciṇṇo tvaṃ sabbakāmehi tapapitoAdubhassa tuvaṃ dubhi taṃ te veraṃ idhāgataṃ Khippaṃ gīvaṃ pasārehi na te dassāmi jīvitaṃBhātuparisaraṃ veraṃ chedayissāmi te siraṃ Ajjhāyako yācayogo āhutaggī ca brāhmaṇoEtehi tīhi ṭhānehi avajjho bhavati brāhmaṇo Duramacari  machasaṃ duramācari  syā  Pekkhavā  machasaṃ syā Sālika  machasaṃ  Piṅgalaṃ  machasaṃ  Pātvarahu  machasaṃ Parivārito  machasaṃ  Aduṭṭhassa  machasaṃ syā  Yācayogi  machasaṃ syā  Hoti machasaṃ   Yaṃ puraṃ dhataraṭṭhassa ogāḷhaṃ yamunaṃ nadiṃJotate sabbasovaṇṇaṃ giriṃ āhacca yāmunaṃ  Tattha te purisavyagghā sodariyā mama bhātaroYathā te tattha vakkhanti tathā hessasi brāhmaṇaSubhagakhaṇḍo Anittarā ittarasampayuttāYaññā ca vedā ca subhoga lokeTadaggarayhaṃ hi vinindamānoJahāti vittañca satañca dhammaṃ  Ajjhenamariyā sabbakāme Vikāsitā cāpasatāni pañcaYo ajjuno balavā bhīmaseno Sahassabāhu asamo paṭhavyāSopi tadā ādahi jātavedaṃ  Yo brāhmaṇo bhojayī dīgharattaṃAntena pāṇena yathānubhāvaṃPasannacitto anumodamānoSubhoga devaññataro ahosi Mahāsanaṃ devamanomavaṇṇaṃYo sappinā asakkhi jetumaggiṃSo yaññatantaṃ varato yajitvāDibbaṃ gatiṃ mucalindajjhagañachiṃ Oghāḷhaṃ  machasaṃ  Jotantaṃ  machasaṃ  Yamunaṃ  machasaṃ Khe  machasaṃ  Atho  machasaṃ  Bhimaseno  machasaṃ   Mahānubhāvo vassasahassajiviYo pabbaji dassaneyyo uḷāroHitvā apariyantarathaṃ sasenaṃRājā dudipopi jagāmaṃ saggaṃ Yo sāgaro sohanti ubhato mukhaṃ Kassa vānena chupitā niddhantā mudukālakaṃ Sobhayanti nalāvantaṃ nabhā vijjurivuggatā Kassa etāni akkhini āyatāni puthuni caKo sobhati visālakkho kassetaṃ uṇaṇajaṃ mukhaṃ Karonti  machasaṃ  Cārudivā  machasaṃ Saṅghāva  machasaṃ  Aṅgaṃ  machasaṃ syā Niccussukkā  machasaṃ  Ubhato  machasaṃ syā Dindimā  machasaṃ syā  Kañavanamaṇidaṇḍāni  machasaṃ suvaṇṇa  syā Okkāmukha vivakkhaṇeVijayañca sunāmañca senāpatimalātakaṃ Tamanupucchi vedeho paccekaṃ brūtha saṃruciṃCātumassa komudajja puṇhaṃ vyapagataṃ tamaṃKāyajja ratiyā rattiṃ viharemu imaṃ utuṃ Lapanājātā  machasaṃ yuddhāya anantabalaporisā Ye te vasaṃ na āyanti vasaṃ upanayāmase Esā mayhaṃ sakādiṭṭhi ajitaṃ ojināmase  Alātassa vaco sutvā sunāmo etadabraviSabbe tuyhaṃ mahārāja avittā vasamāgatā Nikkhittasatthā paccatthā nivātamanuvatatareUttamo ussavo ajja na yuddhaṃ mama ruccati Annaṃ pānañca khajjañca khippaṃ abhiharantu teRamassu deva kāmehi naccagīte suvādite Sunāssa vāco sutvā vijayo etadabraviSabbe kāmā mahārāja niccaṃ tava apaṭṭhitā Na hete dullahā deva tava kāmehi modituṃSadāpi kāmā labbhanti netaṃ cittamataṃ mama Samaṇaṃ brāhoṃ vāpi upāsemu bahussutaṃYo najja vinaye kaṅkhaṃ atthadhammavidu ise Vijayassa vaco sutvā rājā aṅgātimabraviYathā vijayo bhaṇati mayhampeteva ruccati Samaṇaṃ brāhoṃ vāpi upāsemu bahussutaṃYo najja vinaye kaṅkhaṃ atthadhammavidu ise Sabbeva santā karotha matiṃ kaṃ upāsemu paṇḍitaṃKonajja vinaye kaṅkhaṃ atthadhammavidu ise Vedehassa vaco sutvā alāto etadabraviAtthāya migadāyasmiṃ avelo dhirasammato Hataṃ  machasaṃ  Poriso  machasaṃ  Upaniyyāmase  machasaṃ syā Ojiyāmase  machasaṃ syā  Sulabhā  machasaṃ  Guṇo kassapattoyaṃ suto citrakathi gaṇīTaṃ deva payirupāsaya so no kaṅkhaṃ vinessati Alātassa vaco sutvā rājā codesi sārathiṃMigadāyaṃ gamissāma yuttaṃ yānaṃ idānaya  Tassa yānaṃ ayojesuṃ dantaṃ rūpiyapakkharaṃSukkamaṭṭhaparivāraṃ paṇḍaraṃ dosināmukhaṃ Tatrāsuṃ kumudā yuttā cattāro sindhavā hāyāAnilupamasamuppātā sudantā soṇṇamālino Setaṃ chattaṃ setaratho setassā setavijanīVedeho sahamaccehi nīyyaṃ candova sobhatha  Tamannuyāyuṃ bahāvo indakhaggadharā khalīAssapiṭṭhigatā dhīrā narā naravarādhipaṃ So muhuttaṃ va yāyitthā yānā oruyha khattiyoVedeho sahamaccehi patti guṇamupāgami Yopi tattha tadā āsuṃ brāhmaṇibbhā samāgatāNa te apanayī rājā akaṭaṃ bhumimāgate  Tato so mudukābhisiyā muducittakalandakeMudupaccatthate rājā ekamantaṃ upāvisi Nisajja rājā sammodi kathaṃ sārāṇiyaṃ tatoKacci yāpanīyaṃ bhante vātānamavisaggatā  Kacci akasirā vutti labbhati piṇḍayāpanaṃAppabādhovasi kacci cakkhuṃ paribhāyati Taṃ guṇopaṭisammodi vedehaṃ vinaye rataṃYāpaniyaṃ mahārāja sabbametaṃ kadubhayaṃ Payirupāsema  machasaṃ syā  Akiluppasamuppādā  machasaṃ Sobhati  machasaṃ syā  Tamanuyāyiṃsu  machasaṃ Virā  machasaṃ  Muduvitatakasanthate rājā tato pucchi anantarāAtthaṃ dhammañca ñāyañca dhammakamo rathesabho Kathaṃ dhammaṃ care macco mātāpitusu kassapaKathaṃ vacare ācariye puttadāre kathaṃ care Kathaṃ careyya vuddhesu kathaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇeKathañca balakāyasmiṃ kathaṃ jānapade care Kathaṃ dhammaṃ caritvāna pecca gacchati suggatiṃKathañceke adhammaṭṭhā patanti nirayaṃ adho  Vedehassa vaco sutvā kassapo ekadabraviSuṇohi me mahārāja saccaṃ avitatha padaṃ Natthi dhammassa ciṇaṇassa phalaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃNatthi deva paro loko ko tato hi idhāgato Natthi deva pitaro vā kuto mātā kuto pitāNatthi ācariyo nāma adantaṃ ko damesasti Samatulyāni bhūtāni natthī jeṭṭhāpavāyinoNatthi balaṃ vā viriyaṃ vā kuto uṭṭhānaporisaṃ Niyatāni hi bhūtāni yathā goṭaviso tathā Laddhyeṃ labhate macco tattha dānaphalaṃ kutoNatthi machasaṃ vi  Poriso  machasaṃ syā   Santime sassatā kāyā acchejjā avikopino Tejo paṭhavirāpo ca vāyo sukhadukhañcimeJive ca sattime kāyā yesaṃ chettā na vijjati Natthi hantā vā chettā vā haññare vāpi koci naṃAntareneva kāyānaṃ satthāni vitivatatare Yopāyaṃ siramādāya paresaṃ nisitāsināNa so chindati te kāye tattha pāpaphalaṃ kuto Cullāsiti māhakappe sabbe sujjhanti saṃsaraṃAnāgate tambhi kāle saññatopi na sujjhati Caritvāpi bahuṃ bhadraṃ neva sujjhanti nāgetePāpaṃ cepi bahuṃ katvā taṃ khaṇaṃ nātivattare Anupubbena no suddhi kappanaṃ cullasītiyā Niyatiṃ nātivattāma velantamiva sāgaro  Kassapassa vaco sutvā alāto etadabraviYathā bhadanto bhaṇati mayhaṃpeteva ruccati Ahaṃpi purimaṃ jātiṃ dare saṃsaritattanoPiṅgalo nāmahaṃ āsiṃ luddo goghātako pure Bārāṇasiyaṃ phitāya bahuṃ pāpaṃ kataṃ mayāBahu mayhaṃ hatā pāṇā mahisā sukarā ajā Tato cuto idha jāto iddhe senāpatikuleNatthi nūna phalaṃ pāpe sohaṃ na nirayaṃ gato Athettha bījako nāma dāso āsi paḷaccarī Uposathaṃ upavasanto luddakammoNa paṇḍitā tasmiṃ iṇaṃ dadantiNahi āgamo hoti pathāvidhambhā Gatosmi  machasaṃ syā  Acchera  machasaṃ  Pāpanaro  machasaṃ   Dakkhañca posaṃ manujā viditvāUṭṭhāhakaṃ silavantaṃ asipattāvitā dumāAyomayehi tikkhehi naralohitapāyihi Tamānupattaṃ asipattapādapaṃAsihi tikkhehi ca chijjamānaṃ Saṃchinnagantaṃ ruhiraṃ savantaṃKo codaye paraloke sahassaṃ Tato nikkhantamantaṃ taṃ asipattanirayā dukhā Sampatitaṃ cetaraṇiṃ ko taṃ yāceyya taṃ dhanaṃ Kharā khārodikā tattā duggā vetaraṇi nadīAyopokkharasañachantā tikkhapattetahi sandati Tattha sañachintagattaṃ taṃ vuyhantaṃ ruhiramakkhitaṃVetaraññe anālambe ko taṃ yāceyya taṃ dhanaṃ Vedhāmi rukkho viya chijjamānoDisaṃ na jānāmi pamuḷhasaññi Bhayasānutappāmi mahā ca me bhayaṃSutthāna gāthā tava bhāsitā ise Āditte vārimajjhaṃva dipaṃvogherivaṇṇaveAndhakāre pajjoto tvaṃ nosi saraṇaṃ ise  Atthañca dhammañcanusāsa maṃ iseAtitamaddhā aparādhitaṃ mayāĀcikkha me nārada suddhimaggaṃYathā ahaṃ no niraye pateyyaṃ Yathā vyambhe ghosayantu pure tavaKo chāto ko ca tasito ko mālaṃ ko vilepanaṃNānārattānaṃ vatthāṃ ko naggo paridahessati Ko patthe chattamādeti pādukā ca mudu subhāIti sāyañca pato ca ghosayantu pure tava suvaṇṇavālukasanthataṃ Passa tvaṃ paṇaṇasālāyo vibhattā bhāgasomitāNivesane nivese ca sandhibyubhe pathaddhiyo  Pānāgāre ca soṇḍe ca suṇā odaniyāgharāVesī ca gaṇikāyo ca maṇimhi passa nimamitaṃ ca rajake gandhike atha dussikeSuvaṇṇakāre maṇikāre maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ Āḷāriye ca sudace naṭanaṭṭakagāyake Pāṇissare kumbhathunike maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  Passa bheri mutiṅgā ca saṅkhā passa nimmītaṃ Passa pabbatapādesu nānāmigagaṇā bahuSihavyagghavarāhā ca acchakokataracchayo Palasatā ca gavajā ca mahisā rohitā rurūPhaṇeyyā ca varāhā ca gaṇino niṅkasukarā Kadalimigā bahu citrā pacchatoKuruyo jambudipañca maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ Passa candāñca suriyañca obhāsente catuddisāSineruṃ anupariyanne maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ Sineruṃ himavantañca sāgarañca mahiddhikaṃ Cattāro ca mahārāja maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ Ārāme vanagumbe ca pāṭiye ca siluccayeRamme kimpurisākiṇṇe maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ Phārusakaṃ cittalataṃ missakaṃ nandanaṃ vanaṃVejayantañca pāsādaṃ maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ Sudhammaṃ rajatāmayāIndagopakavaṇṇābhā tāva dissanti tiṃsati Dasettha kāḷiyo cha ca mañjeṭṭhā paṇṇavisatiMissā bandhukapupphehi nīluppalavicittitā Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampannaṃ accimantaṃ pabhassaraṃOdhisuṅkaṃ sahakekakehiPassantu no te asaṭhena yuddhaṃNa no sabhāyaṃ na kāroti kiñci  Te pāvisuṃ akkhamadena mattāRājā kurūnaṃ puṇṇako cāpi yakkhoRājā kaliṃ vicinaṃ aggahesiKaṭamaggahī puṇṇako nāma yakkho samāgateRaññaṃ sakāse sakhinañca majjheAjesi yakkho naraviriyaseṭṭhaṃTatthappanādo tumulo babhūva  Jayo mahārāja parājayo caĀyuhataṃ aññatarassa hotiJaninda jinosi varaṃ dhananaJito ca me khippamavākarohi Hatthi gavāssā maṇikuṇḍalā caYaṃ cāpi mayhaṃ ratanaṃ pathavyāGaṇhāhi kaccāna varaṃ dhanānaṃĀdāya yenicchasi tena gaccha Hatthi gavāssā maṇikuṇḍalā caYañcāpi tuyhaṃ ratanaṃ pathavyāTesaṃ varo vidhuro nāma kattāSo me jito taṃ me avākarohi Antā ca me so saraṇaṃ gati caDīpo ca leṇo ca parāyano caAsantuleyyo mama so dhanenaPāṇena me sadiso esa kattā  Ciraṃ vivādo mama tuyhamassaKāmañca pucchāma tameva gantvāEsova no vicaratu etamatthaṃYaṃ vakkhati hotu kathā ubhinnaṃ Addhā hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi na ca māṇava sāhasaṃTameva gantvā pucchāma tena tussāmubho janā Saccannu devā vidahu kurūnaṃDhamme ṭhitaṃ vidhuraṃ nāmamaccaṃDāsosi rañño udavāsi ñātīVidhuroti saṅkhā katamāsi loke  Āmāya dāsāmi bhavanti hekeDhanena kītāpi bhavanti dāsāSayampi bheke upayanti dāsāBhayā paṇuntāpi bhavanti dāsāEte narānaṃ caturova dāsā Tuyhañcassa  machasaṃ syā  Tathā  machasaṃ vi syā  Addhā hi yonito ahampi jato bhavo ca rañño abhavo ca raññoDāsāhaṃ devassa parampi gantvāDhammena maṃ māṇava tuyhaṃ dajjā Ayampi dutiyo vijayo mamajjaPuṭṭho hi kattā vivarittha pañhaṃAdhammarūpo vata rājaseṭṭhoSubhāsitaṃ nānujānāsi mayhaṃ  Evaṃ ce no so vivarettha pañhaṃDāsohamasmi na ca khosmi bandhave Kammannaṃ saṃvidhetvāna ācikkhitvā ghare dhanaṃNidhiñca iṇadānañca puṇṇaṃ etadabravi Avasī tuvaṃ mayha tīhaṃ agāreKatāni kiccāni gharesu mayhaṃAnusāsitā putatadārā mayā caKaroma kaccāna yathā matiṃ te  Sace hi katte anusāsitā tePuttā ca dārā ca anujivino caHandehi dāni taramānarūpoDīgho hi addhāpi ayaṃ puratthā Asambhitova gaṇhāhi ājāniyassa vāladhiṃIdaṃ pacchimakaṃ tuyhaṃ jivalokassa dassanaṃ Sohaṃ kissa nu bhāyissaṃ yassa me natthi dukkataṃKāyena vācā manasā yena gaccheyya duggatiṃ So assarājā vidhuraṃ vahantoPakkāmi vehāsayamantalikkheSākhāsu selesu assajjamanoKāḷāgiriṃ khippamupāgamāsi Ājāneyyasasa  machasaṃ   Itthi sahasasaṃ bhariyānaṃ dāsisattasatāni caKhāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ yakkho brāhmaṇavaṇṇe vidhuraṃ ādāya gacchatiOrodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāBāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ yakkho brāhmaṇavaṇṇe vidhuraṃ ādāya gacchati Itthi sahasasaṃ bhariyānaṃ dāsisattasatāni caVejayantañca pāsādaṃ maṇimhi passa nimitaṃOrodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāBāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ paṇḍito so kuhiṃ gato  Sace so sattarattena paṇḍito nāgamisastiSabbe aggiṃ pavekkhāma natthattho jivitena no Paṇḍito ca viyatto ca vibhāvi ca vicakkhaṇoKhippaṃ mocessatattānaṃ mā paduṭṭhacittoAsaṃvutasmiṃ jagatippadeseAdhosiraṃ dhārayi kātiyāno So lambamāno narake papāteMahabbhaye lomahaṃse viduggeAsantasaṃ kurūnaṃ kattaseṭṭhoIccabravī puṇṇakaṃ nāma yakkhaṃ Khippaṃ mociya attānaṃ  machasaṃ  Cetanatā  machasaṃ Mamatthi  machasaṃ syā  Assanatasanto  machasaṃ syā vi  Ariyācakāsosi anariyarūpoAsaññato saññatasantikāsoAccābhitaṃ kammaṃ karosi ludraṃBhāve ca te kusalaṃ natthi kiñci Yaṃ maṃ papātasmiṃ papātumicchasiKonu tavattho maraṇena mayhaṃAmānusasseva te ajja vaṇṇoĀcikkha me tvaṃ katamāsi devatā  Yadi te suto puṇṇako nāma yakkhoRañño kuverassa hi so sajivo Bhumindharo varuṇo nāma nāgoBrahā sucī vaṇṇabaluppanno Tassānujaṃ dhitaraṃ kāmayāmiIrandatiṃ nāma sā nāgakaññāTassā sumajjhāya piyāya hetuPatārayiṃ tuyha vadhāya dhira Māheva tvaṃ yakkha ahosi muḷhoNaṭṭhā bahu duggahitena lokāKinne sumajjhāya piyāya kiccaṃ maraṇena me iṅgha suṇoma sabbaṃ Mahānubāvassa mahoragassaDhitukāmo ñātibhatohamasmi Taṃ yācamānaṃ sasuro acocaYathā maṃ aññiṃsu sukāmanītaṃ  Dajjemu kho te sutanuṃ sunettaṃSucimbhitaṃ candanalittagattaṃSace tuvaṃ hadayaṃ paṇḍitassaDhammena laddhā idhamāharesiEtena vittena kumāri labbhāNāññaṃ dhanaṃ uttariṃ patthayāma Evaṃ na muḷhosmi suṇohi katteNa cāpi me duggahitthi kiñciHadayena te dhammaladdhena nāgāIrandatiṃ nāgakaññaṃ dadanti Tavajja  machasaṃ syā  Te  machasaṃ syā Sajibbo  machasaṃ syā  Sumicchā  machasaṃ Sumicchāya  machasaṃ  Haṭo  machasaṃ  Tasmā ahaṃ tuyha vadhāya yuttoEvaṃ mamattho maraṇena tuyhaṃIdheva taṃ narake pātayitvāHanatvāna taṃ hadayaṃ ādiyissaṃ  Khippaṃ mamaṃ uddhara kātiyānaHadayena me yadi te atthiYe kecime sādhunarassa dhammāSabbeva te pātukaromi ajja Sa puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattaseṭṭhaṃNagamuddhani khippaṃ patiṭṭhapetvāAsasatthamāsinaṃ samekkhiyānaParipucchi kattāraṃ anomapaññaṃ Samuddhaṭo mesi tuvaṃ papātāHadayena te ajja mamatthi kiccaṃYe kecime sādhunarassa dhammāSabbeva me pātukarohi ajja Samuddhaṭo tyasmi ahaṃ papātāHadayena me nadi te atthi kiccaṃYe kecime sādhunarassa dhammāSabbeva me pātukarohi ajja  Yātānuyāyi ca bhavāhi māṇavaAddañca pāṇiṃ parivajjayassuMā cassu mittesu kadāci dubhīMā ca vasaṃ asatīnaṃ nigacche Kathannu yātaṃ anuyāyi hotiAddañca pāṇiṃ dahate kathaṃ soAsati ca kā ko pana mittadubbhoAkkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ Asanthutaṃ nopi ca diṭṭhipubbaṃYo āsanenāpi nimantayeyyaTasseva atthaṃ puriso kareyyaYātānuyāyīti tamāhu paṇḍitā Tusmi  machasaṃ  Allañca  machasaṃ syā  Assatthataṃ  syā asandhavaṃ machasaṃ  Yassekarattimpi ghare vaseyyaYatthannapānaṃ puriso labhetha Na tassa pāpaṃ manasāpi cetayeAddañcapāṇiṃ dahate mittadubbho Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vāNa tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubbo hi pāpako Puṇṇampi cetaṃ paṭhaviṃ dhanenaDajjatthiyā puriso sammatāyaLaddā khaṇaṃ atimaññeyya tampiTāsaṃ vasaṃ asatinaṃ na gacche Evaṃ kho yātaṃ anuyāyi hotiAddañca pāṇiṃ dahate punevaṃAsatī ca sā so pana mittadubbhoSo dhammiyo hohi jahassu adhammaṃSādhunaradhammakaṇḍaṃ  Avasiṃ ahaṃ tuyha tīhaṃ agāreAntena pānena upaṭṭhitosmiMitto mamāsi visajāmahaṃ taKāmaṃ gharaṃ uttamapañña gaccha  Api hāyatu nāgakulassa atthoAlampi me nāgakaññāya hotuSo tvaṃ sakeneva subhāsitenaMuttosi me ajja vadhāya pañña Handa tuvaṃ yakkha mamampi nehiSasuraṃ nu te atthaṃ mayī carassuMayampi nāgādhipatiṃ vimānaṃDakkhemu nāgassa adiṭṭhapubbaṃ Yaṃ ve narassa ahitāya assaNa taṃ pañño arahati dasasanāyaAtha kena vaṇṇena amittagāmaṃTuvampicchasi uttamapañña anatuṃ Labheyya  machasaṃ  Cittaye  machasaṃ syā Alalañca  syā adubbhi pāṇaṃ  machasaṃ adubbhapāṇiṃ  sīmu aṭṭhakathā Allañca  machasaṃ syā  Visajjāmaha taṃ  syā visajjemahantaṃ  machasaṃ  Addhā pajānāmi ahmapi etaṃNa taṃ pañño arahati dasasanāyaPāpañca me natthi kataṃ kuhiñciTasmā na saṅke maraṇāgamāya  Handa ca ṭhānaṃ atulānubhāvaṃMayā sahā dakkhisi ehi katteYatthacchati naccagītehi nāgoRājā yathā vessavaṇo naliññaṃ Taṃ nāgakaññācaritaṃ gaṇenaNikiḷitaṃ niccamaho ca rattiṃPahutamālyaṃ bahupupphachannaṃObhāsati vijjurivantalikkhe Antena pānena upetarūpaṃNacceti gītehi ca vāditehiParipuraṃ kaññāhi alaṅkatāhiUpasobhati vatthapiḷandhanena So puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattaseṭṭhaṃNisidayi pacchato āsanasmiṃĀdāya kattāraṃ anomapaññaṃUpānayī bhavanaṃ nāgarañño Patvāna ṭhānaṃ atulānubhāvaṃAṭṭhāsi kattā pacchato puṇṇakassaSāmaggipekkhī pana nāgarājāPubbeva jāmātaramajjhabhāsatha  Yannu tuvaṃ agamā maccalokaṃAnvesamāno hadayaṃ paṇḍitassaKacci samiddhena idhānupattoĀdāya kattāraṃ anomapaññaṃ Ayaṃ hi so āgato yaṃ tvamicchasiDhammena laddho mama dhammapāloTaṃ passatha sammukhā bhāsamānaṃSukho bhave sappurisehi saṅgamoKāḷāgirikaṇḍaṃ Vassavano  machasaṃ  Kaḷaññaṃ  machasaṃ  Bahuttamallaṃ  machasaṃ Saccannaṃ  machasaṃ  Vasanaṃ  machasaṃ  Taṃ passa dhammaṃ samukhā  machasa  Adiṭṭhapubbaṃ disvāna macco maccubhayaddito Vyambhito nābhivādeti nayidaṃ paññavatāmiva  Nacambhi vyambhito nāga naca maccubhayadditoNa vajjho abhivadeyya vajjhaṃ vā nibhivādaye Kathaṃ nu abhivāseyya abhivādāpayetha veYaṃ naro hantumiccheyya taṃ kammaṃ na upapajjati Evametaṃ yathā brūsi saccaṃ bhāsasi paṇḍitaNa vajjho abhivāseyya vajjhaṃ vā nābhivādaye Kathaṃ nu abhivāseyya abhivādāpayetha veYaṃ naro hantumiccheyya taṃ kammaṃ na upapajjati Asassataṃ sassataṃ nu tavayidaṃIddhījutī balaviriyupapattiPucchāmi taṃ nāgarājetamatthaṃKathannu te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ Adhicca laddhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ teSayaṃ kataṃ udāhu dinnaṃAkkhāhi me nāgarājetamatthaṃYatheva te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ  Nādhicca laddhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ meNa sayaṃ kataṃ napi devehi dinnaṃSakehi kamemhi apāpakehiPuññehi me laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ Kiṃ te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃKissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipākoIdadhijuti balaviriyupapattiIdaṃ ca te nāga mahāvimānaṃ Ahañca bhariyā ca manussalokeSaddhā ubho dānapatī ahumahāOpānabhūtaṃ me gharaṃ tadāsiSantappitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca Bhayaṭṭito  machasaṃ syā  No  sīmu  Nāpi  machasaṃ  Mālañca gandhañca vilepanañcaPadīpiyā seyyamupassayañcaAcchādanaṃ sayanaṃ annapānaṃSakkacca dānāni adamaha tattha Taṃ me vataṃ taṃ pana brahmacariyaṃTassa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipākoIdadhijuti balaviriyupapatti idañca me dhira mahāvimonaṃ  Evaṃ ce te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃJānāsi puññānaṃ phalupapattiTasmāhi dhammaṃ cara appamattoYathā vimānaṃ puna māvasesi Nayidha santi samaṇabrāhmaṇā vāYesannapānāni dademu katteAkkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃYathā vimānaṃ puna māvasema Bhogī hi te santi idhupapantāPuttā ca dārā anujivino caTesu tuvaṃ vacasā kammanā caAsampaduṭṭho ca bhavāhi niccaṃ sameccaVindeyya poso sukhamāturopi Addhā sataṃ bhāsasi nāga dhammaṃAnuttaraṃ atthapadaṃ suciṇṇaṃEtādisiyāsu hi āpadāsuPaññāyate mādisānaṃ viseso Dukkhopaṇitopi  machasaṃ  Akkhehi no tāyaṃ mudhā nu asāhasena Mahorago attamano udaggoSutvāna dhirassa subhāsitāniHatthe gahetvāna anomapaññaṃPāvekkhi bhariyāya tadā sakāse Yena tvaṃ vimale paṇḍu yena bhattaṃ na ruccatiNa ca me tādiso vaṇṇo ayameso tamonudo Yassa te hadayenattho āgatāyaṃ pabhaṅkaroTassa vākyaṃ nisāmehi dullabhaṃ dasasnaṃ puna Disvāna te vimalā bhuripaññaṃDasaṅguliṃ pañajaliṃ paggahetvāHaṭṭhena bhāvena patītarūpāIcchabravi Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāBahuṃ antañca pānañca paṇḍitasasābhihārayuṃ Hatthāruhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā Bahuṃ annañca pānañca paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ  Samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatāBahuṃ annañca pānañca paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ Bahujjano pasantosi disvā paṇḍitamāgatePaṇḍitamhi anuppatte celukkhepo avatatthāti Vidhurapaṇḍitajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ Rahā  machasaṃ syā  Pattikārikā  vi Tālāhi  machasaṃ vi  Bahujano  machasaṃ Hatthārohā  machasaṃ vi syā  Pavatatathāti  machasaṃ syā  Ummaggajātakaṃ  Sabbasaṃhārako natthi suddhaṃ kaṅgu pavāyatiAlikaṃ bhāsatayaṃ dhutti saccamāhu mahallikāSattadārakapañhā  Haṃsi tuvaṃ evaṃ maññesi seyyoPuttena pitāti rājaseṭṭhaHandassatarassa te ayaṃAssatarassa hi gadrabho pitāGadrabhapañhoEkunavīsatipañhā niṭṭhitā  Nāyaṃ pure unnamati toraṇagge kakaṇṭakoMahosadha vijānāhi kena thaddho kakaṇṭako Aladdhapubbaṃ laddhāna addhamāsaṃ kakaṇṭakoAtimaññati rājānaṃ vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃKakaṇṭaka pañho  Itthi siyā rūpavati sā ca sīlavati siyāPuriso taṃ na iccheyya sadadhāsi mahosadha  Sadadhāmi mahārāja puriso dubbhago siyāSiri ca kālakaṇṇi ca na samonti kudācanaṃSurikālakaṇṇi pañho  Yesaṃ na kadāci bhūtapubbaṃSakkhiṃ santapadampi imasmiṃ lekeJātā amittā duve sahāyāPaṭisandhāya caranti kissa hetu Yadi me ajja pātarāsakālePañhaṃ na sakkuṇeyyātha vantumetaṃRaṭṭhā pabbājayissāmi vo sabbeNa hi mattho duppaññajātikehi Dubhago  machasaṃ vi  Na samanti  machasaṃ  Sakkuṇetha  sīmu sakkuṇatha syā Pabbājayissāmi  sīmu   Mahājanasamāgamambhi ghoreJanakolahalasamāgamambhi jateVikkhittamanā anekacintāPañhaṃ na sakkuṇoma vattumetaṃ Ekaggacittā ekamekāRahasigatā atthaṃ nicintayitvā Paviveke sammasitvāna dhīrāAtha vakkhanti janinda atthametaṃ  UggaputtarājaputtiyānaUrabbhamaṃsaṃ piyaṃ manāpaṃNa te sunakhassa adenti maṃsaṃAtha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa Cammaṃ vibhananti eḷakassaAssapiṭṭhattharaṇasukhassa hetuNa te sunakhassa attharattiAtha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa  Āvellitasiṅgiko hi meṇḍoNa sunakhassa visāṇāni atthiTiṇabhakkho maṃsabhojano caAtha meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa Tiṇamāsi pālasamāsi meṇḍoNa sukho tiṇamāsi no palāsaṃGaṇheyya suṇo sasaṃ khiḷāraṃAtha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa Aḍḍhaṭṭhapādo catuppadassa meṇḍo aṭṭhanakho adissamānoChādiyaṃ āharati ayaṃ imassaMaṃsaṃ āharati ayaṃ amussa Pāsādagato videhaseṭṭhoVitihāraṃ aññamaññabhojanānaṃAddakkhi kira sakkhi taṃ janindoBhobhukkassa ca puṇṇamukhasasa cetaṃ Atthāni cittayitvā  machasaṃ syā  Aṭṭhaḍḍha  machasaṃ syā  Bobhukkassa  simu   Lābhā vata me anapparūpāYassa me edisā paṇḍitā kulambhiGambhiragataṃ nipuṇamatthaṃPaṭivijjhanti subhāsitena dhīrā Assatarirathañca ekamekaṃPhitaṃ gāmavarañca ekamekaṃSabbaṃ vo dammi paṇḍitānaṃParamappanitano subhāsitenātiDvādasanipāte  meṇḍakapañhaṃ  Paññāyupetaṃ siriyā vihīnaṃYasassinañcāpi apetapaññaṃPucchāmi taṃ senaka etamatthaṃKamettha seyyo kusalā vadanti Dhīrā ca bālā ca bhatva janindaSippupapannā ca asippino caSujātimantopi ajātimassaYassasino pessakarā bhavantiEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPañño nihīno sirimāva seyye Tavampi pucchāmi anomapañña mahosadha kevaladhammadassiBālaṃ yasassiṃ paṇḍitaṃ appahogaṃKamettha seyyo kusalā vadanti  Pāpāni kammāni karoti bāloIdhameva seyyo iti maññamānoIdhalokadassi paralokaṃ adassiUbhayattha bālo kalimaggahesiEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññova seyyo na yasassī bālo Na sippametaṃ vidadhāti bhogaṃNa bandhavā na sarīrāvakāsoPasseḷamugaṃ sukhamedhamānaṃSiri hi naṃ bhajate gorimanadaṃEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPañño nihino sirimāva seyyo Pañhassa  machasaṃ syā   Laddhā sukhaṃ majjati appapaññoDukkhena phuṭṭhopi samohametiĀgantunā sukhadukkhena phuṭṭhoPavedhati vāricarova ghammeEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo Dumaṃ yathā sāluphalaṃ araññeSamantato samabhicaranti pakkhiEvampi aḍḍhaṃ sadhanaṃ sabhogaṃBahujjano bhajati atthahetuEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva nihino sirimāva seyyo   Na sādhu balavā bālo sāhasaṃ vindate dhanaṃKandantameva dummedhaṃ kaḍḍhanti niraye bhusaṃEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo Yā kāci najjo gaṅgamabhissavantiSabbāva tā nāmagottaṃ jahantiGaṅgā samuddaṃ paṭipajjamānāNa khāyate iddhiparo hi lokoEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva nihīno sirimāva seyyo Yametamakkhā udadhiṃ mahantaṃSamanti najjo sabbakālaṃ asaṅkhaṃSo sāgaro niccamuḷāravegoVelaṃ na acceti hāsamudedā Evampi bālassa pajappitāniPaññaṃ na acceti siri kadāciEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  Asaññato cepi paresamatthaṃBhaṇāti santhānagato yasassiTasseva taṃ rūhati ñātimajjheSiri hi naṃ kārayate na paññāEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva nibhino sirimāva seyyo Dhuva phalaṃ  machasaṃ  Kandantametaṃ  machasaṃ  Iddhi paññopi  machasaṃ Masaṅkhyaṃ  machasaṃ  Saṇṭhānagato  syā  Parassa vā antano vāpi hetuBālo musā bhāsati appapaññoSo nindito hoti sabhāya majjhePeccāpi so duggatigāmi hotiEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  Atthampi ce bhāsati bhuripaññoAnāḷhiyo appadhano daḷiddoNa tassa taṃ rūbhati ñātimajjheSiri ca paññāṇavato na hotiEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva nihino sirimāva seyyo Parassa vā attano vāpi hetuNa bhāsati alikaṃ bhuripaññoSo pujito hoti sabhāya majjhePeccañca so suggatigāmi hotiEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo Hatthigavassā maṇikuṇḍalā caNāriyo ca iddhesu kulesu jātāSabbāva tā upabhogā bhavantiIddhassa posassa aniddhimantoEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo Asaṃvihitakammantaṃ bālaṃ dummantamattinaṃSiri jahati dummedhaṃ jiṇṇaṃva urago tavaṃEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  Pañca paṇḍitā mayaṃ bhadanteSabbe pañjalikā upaṭṭhitāTvaṃ no abhibhuyya issarosiSakko bhūtapatīva devarājāEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva nihīno sirimāva seyyo Pacchāpi  machasaṃ syā  Anāliyo  machasaṃ syā Pacchāpi  machasaṃ syā  Thiyo  machasaṃ Dummedha  machasaṃ  Iriyasi  vi  Dāsova paññassa yasassi bāloAtthesu jātesu tathāvidhesuYaṃ paṇḍito nipuṇaṃ saṃcidhetiSammohamāpajjati tattha baloEtampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmiPaññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  Addhā hi paññāva sataṃ pasatthāKantā siri bhogaratā manussāÑāṇañca buddhānamatulyarūpaṃPaññaṃ na acceti siri kadāci Yaṃ taṃ apucchimbha akittayi noMahosadha kevaladhammadassīGavaṃ sahassaṃ usabhañca nāgaṃĀjaññayutte ca rathe dasa imePañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭhoDadāmi te gāmavarāni soḷayaVisatinipāte sirimanda pañho  Yena sattu bilaṅgā caDviguṇapalāso ca pupphitoYenādāmi tena vadāmiEsa maggo yavamajjhakassaEtaṃ chattapathaṃ vijānahiChattapathapañho Hanti hatthehi pādehi mukhañca parisumbhatiSace rāja piyo hoti kaṃ tenamabhipassati   Ko nu santambhi pajjote aggipariyesanaṃ caraṃAddakkhi rattiṃ khajjotaṃ jātavedaṃ amaññatha Svāssa gomayacuṇṇāni abhimatthaṃ tiṇāni caViparitāya saññāya nāsakkhi sañajaletace  Evampi anupāyena atthaṃ na labhate mago Visāṇato gavaṃ dohaṃ yattha khiraṃ na vindati Kanetana tvābhipassati  machasaṃ  Pajjaletavenārada pajjeletave  machasaṃ sya Mugo  syā  Vividhehi upāyehi atthaṃ papponti māṇavāNiggahena amittānaṃ mitatānaṃ paggahena ca Seṇimokkhopalābhena vallabhānaṃ nāyena caJagatiṃ jagatipālā avasanti vasundharaṃKhajjopaṇaka pañho  Sacca kira tvampi bhuripaññoYā tādisi siri dhiti muti caNa tāyate bhāvavasupanītaṃYo yāvakaṃ bhuñjasi appasupaṃ Sukhaṃ dukkhena paripācayantoKālakālaṃ vicinaṃ chandachanto Atthassa dvārāni avāpurantoTenāhaṃ tussāmi yavodanne Kālañca ñatvā abhijihanāyaMantehi atthaṃ paripācayitvāVijambhissaṃ sihavijambhitāniTāyiddhiyā dakkhasi maṃ punāpi  Sukhī hi eke karonti pāpaṃAvaṇṇasaṃsaggabhayā punekePahu samāno vipulatthivintiKiṃ kāraṇā me na karosi dukkhaṃ  Na paṇḍitā antasukhassa hetuPāpāni kammāni samācarantiDukkhena puṭṭhā khalitattāpi santāChandā ca dosā na jahanti dhammaṃ Yena kenaci vaṇṇena mudunā dārunena vāUddhare dinamantānaṃ pacchā dhammaṃ samācare Seni mokkhupalābhena  machasaṃ sonāmokkhapalābhena  syā Atibhuripañña  machasaṃ  Bhuñji  machasaṃ  Kālānakālaṃ  machasaṃ Channa  machasaṃ  Vijambhisaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Sukhipihete  machasaṃ syā Khalitāpi  machasaṃ  Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vāNa tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubbho hi pāpako Yassā hi dhammaṃ manujo vijaññāYecassa kaṅkhaṃ vinayanti santoTaṃ hissa dipañca parāyaṇañcaNa tena mittaṃ jarayetha pañño Alaso gihī kāmabhogi na sādhuAsaññato pabbajito na sādhuRājā na sādhu anisammakārīYo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu  Nisamma khattiyo kayirā nānisamma disampatiNisammakārino rāja yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhatiBhuripañho Hanti hatthehi pādehi mukhañca parisumbhatiSa ce rāja piyo hoti kaṃ tena mabhipassasi  Akkosati yathākāmaṃ āgamañcassa na icchatiSa ce rājā piyo hoti taṃ tena mabhipassasi Abbhakkhāti abhutena alikena mabhisāraye sa ce rāja piyo hoti kaṃ tenamabhipassasi  Haraṃ antañca pānañca vatthasenāsanāni caAññadatthu harā santā te ve rāja piyā honti kaṃ tenamabhipassasiDevatāpucchita pañha  Pañca paṇḍitā samāgatāPañehā me paṭibhāti taṃ suṇāthaNindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vāKassevāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ Yassa hi  machasaṃ  Mitti jiyetha  machasaṃ mettiṃ  syā  Tvaṃ no ācikarohi bhumipālaBhattā bhārasaho tuvaṃ vadetaṃTava chandañca ruciñca sammasitvāAtha vakkhanti janinda pañca dhīrā  Yā sīlavati anaññadheyyāBhattucchandavasānugā piyā manāpāNindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vāBhariyāyāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ Yo kicchagatasasa āturassaSaraṇaṃ hoti gati parāyaṇañcaNindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vāSakhinovāvikaroyya guyhamatthaṃ Jeṭṭho atha majjhimo kaṇiṭṭhoSo ce silasamāhito ṭhitattoNindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vāBhātuvāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ Yo ve pitubhadayassa paddhaguAnujāto pitaraṃ anomapaññoNindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vāPuttassāvīkareyya guyhamatthaṃ Mātā dipādā janindaseṭṭhaYo taṃ poseti chandasā piyenaNindiyamatthaṃ saṃsiyaṃ vāMātuyāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ  Guyhassa hi guyhameva sādhuNa hi guyhassa pasatthamāvikammaṃAnipphādāya saheyya dhīroNipphantattho yathāsukhaṃ bhaṇeyya  Kinnu tvaṃ vimano rājaseṭṭhaDipadinda vacanaṃ suṇoma netaṃ Kiṃ cintayamāno dummanosiNuna deva aparādho atthi mayhaṃ Tvaṃ ācikarohi  machasaṃ syā  Yā  machasaṃ syā Rucini  machasaṃ syā  Anipphannatāya  machasaṃ syā Vagganti  machasaṃ  Dvipada janinda  machasaṃ Anaññatheyyā  machasaṃ syā  Metaṃ  machasaṃ  Pañño vajjho mahosadhotiĀṇatto mevadhāya bhuripaññoTaṃ cintayanto dummanosmiNa hi devi aparādho atthi tuyhaṃ  Abhidosagato idāni esiKiṃ sutvā kimāsaṃkate mano teKo te kimavoca bhuripaññaIṅgha taṃ vacanaṃ suṇoma brūhi metaṃ Pañño vajjho mahosadhotiYadi te mantayitaṃ janinda dosaṃBhariyāya rahogato asaṃsiGuyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ  Yaṃ sālavanasmiṃ senakoPāpakammaṃ akāsi asabbhirūpaṃSakhinova rahogāto asaṃsiGuyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ Pukkusapurisassa te janinda uppanno rogo arājayutto  bhātucca rahogato asaṃsiGuyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ Ābādhoyaṃ asabbhirūpoKāvindo naradevena phuṭṭhoPuttassa rabogato asaṃsiGuyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ  Aṭṭhavaṅkaṃ maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃSakko te adadā pitāmahassaDevindassa gataṃ tadajja hatthaṃMātucca rahogato asaṃsiGuyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ Guyhassa hi guyhameva sādhuNa hi guyhasasa pasatthamāvikammaṃAnipphādāya saheyya dhīroNippannattho yathāsukhaṃ bhaṇeyya Vinatayamāno  machasaṃ syā vi  Ehisi  machasaṃ syā  Ki saṅkate  machasaṃ syā Arājapatto  machasaṃ syā  Ābādhāyaṃ  machasaṃ syā Anipphannatāya  machasaṃ  Na guyhamatthaṃ vivareyya rakkheyya naṃ yathā nidhiṃNa hi pātukato sādhu guyho attho pajānatā Thiyā guyhaṃ na saṃseyya amittassa ca paṇḍitoYo cāmisena saṃbhiro hadayattheno ca yo naro Guyhamatthamasambuddhaṃ sambodhayati yo naroMantabhedabhayā tassa dasabhuto titikkhati Yāvanto purisassatthaṃ guyhaṃ jānanti mantinaṃTāvanto tassa ubbegā tasmā guyhaṃ na vissaje  Vivicca bhāseyya divā rahassaṃRattiṃ giraṃ nātivela pamuñceUpassutikā hi suṇanti mantaṃTasmā manto khippamupeti bhedaṃVisatinipāte pañcapaṇḍitapañehā  Pañcālo sabbasenāya brahmadatto samāgatoSāyaṃ pañcāliyā senā appameyyā sahosadha Piṭṭhimatī pattimati sabbasaṅgāmekovidāOhārini saddavati bherisaṅkhappabodhanā Lohavijjālaṅkārābhā dhajini vāmarohiṇiSippiyehi susampannā surehi suppatiṭṭhitā Dasettha paṇḍitā āhu bhuripaññā rabhogamā Mātā ekādasī rañño pañcāliyaṃ pasāsati  Athetthekasataṃ khatyā anuyuttā yasassinoAcchinnaraṭṭhā byathitā pañcālīnaṃ vasaṃgatā Alaṅkārā  machasaṃ syā  Vijini  machasaṃ  Rabhogatā  machasaṃ  Paṃvadā takkarā rañño akāmā piyabhāṇinoPañcālamanuyāyanti akāmā vino gatā Tāya senāya mithilā tisandhi parivāritāRājadhāni videbhānaṃ samantā parikhaññati Uddhaṃ tārakajātāva samantā parivāritāMahosadha vijānāhi kathaṃ mokkho bhavissati  Pāde deva pasārehi bhuñja kāme ramassu caHitvā pañcāliyaṃ senā brahmadatto palāyati  Rājā panthavakāmo te ratanāni pavecchatiĀgacchantu tato dutā mañajukā piyabhāṇino Bhāsantu mudukā vācā yā vācā paṭinanditāPañcālā ca videhā ca uho ekā bhavantu te  Kathannu kevaṭṭa mahosadhenaSamāgamo āsi tadiṅgha brūhiKacci te paṭinijjhanto kacci tuṭṭho mahosadho Anariyarūpo puriso janindaAsammodako thaddho asabbhirūpoYathā mugo ca badhiro ca na kiñcatthaṃ abhāsatha Addhā idaṃ mantapadaṃ sududdasaṃAttho suddho naraviriyena diṭṭhoTathā hi kāyo mama sampavedhatiHitvā sayaṃ ko parahatthamessati  Channaṃ hi ekāva matī sametiYe paṇḍitā uttamabhuripattāYānaṃ ayānaṃ athavāpi ṭhānaṃMahosadha tvampi matiṃ karohi  Jānāsi kho rāja mahānubhāvoMahabbalo cuḷanibrahmadattoRājā ca taṃ icchati kāraṇatthaṃMigaṃ yathā okacarena luddo Rājadhāniṃ  machasaṃ  Palāyiti  machasaṃ  Mudutā  machasaṃ Naravirena  machasaṃ syā  Vedhate  machasaṃ  Magaṃ  machasaṃ Okkacarena  machasaṃ  Yathāpi maccho khaḷisaṃ vaṅkaṃ maṃsena chāditaṃĀmagiddho na jānāti maccho maraṇamattano Evameva tuvaṃ rāja cuḷaniyassa dhitaraṃKāmagiddho na jānasi macchova maraṇamatatano Sace gacchasi pañcālaṃ khippamantaṃ jahissasiMigaṃ pathānupannaṃva mahannaṃ bhayamessati  Mayameva bālambase eḷamugāYe uttamatthāni tayī lapimbhaKimeva tvaṃ naṅgalakoṭivaddhoAtthāni jānāsi yathāpi aññe Imaṃ gale gahetvāna nāsetha vijitā mamaYo me ratanalābhassa antarāyāya bhāsati  Tato ca so apakkamma vedehassa upantikāAtha āmantayī dutaṃ māḍharaṃ suvapaṇḍataṃ Ehi samma haripakkha veyyāvaccaṃ karohi meAtthi pañcālarājassa sāḷikā sayanapālikā Taṃ pattharena pucchassu sā hi sabbassa kovidāSā tesaṃ sabbaṃ jānāti rañño ca kosiyassa ca Āmoti so paṭissutvā māḍharo suvapaṇḍitoAgamāsi haripakkho sāḷikāya upantikaṃ Tato ca kho so gantvāna māḍharo suvapaṇḍitoAtha āmantayi sugharaṃ sāḷikaṃ mañajubhāṇikaṃ Kacci te sughare khamanīyaṃ kacci vesse anāmayaṃKacci te madhunā lājā labbhate sughare tava Kusalañceva me samma atho samma anāmayaṃAtho me madhunā lājā labbhate suvapaṇḍite Cuḷaneyyassa  machasaṃ  Panthānu  machasaṃ vi  Vaḍḍho  machasaṃ Mādharaṃ  machasaṃ mādhuraṃ  syā  Haritapakkha  machasaṃ syā Bandhanena  machasaṃ pattharane  syā satthacena  syā  Vese  machasaṃ syā  Kuto nu samma āgamma kassa vā pahito tuvaṃNa ca mesi ito pubbe diṭṭho vā yadi vā suto  Ahosiṃ sivirājassa pāsādo sayanapālakoTato so dhammiko rājā baddhe mocesi bandhaṇā  Tassa mekā dutiyāsi sāḷikā ñajubhāṇikāTaṃ tattha avadhi seno pekkhato sughare mama Tassā kāmā hi sammatto āgatosmi tavantikeSace kareyyasi okāsaṃ ubhatyāva vasāmese  Suvoca suviṃ kāmeyya sāḷiko pana sāḷikaṃSuvassa sāḷikāya ca saṃvāso hoti kidiso Yaṃ yaṃ kāmi kāmayati api caṇḍālikāmapiSabbhi sadiso hoti natthi kāme asādiso Atthi jambāvati nāma mātā sivissa rājinoSā bhariyā vāsudevassa kaṇhassa mahesī piyā  Rathāvati kimpurisi sāpi vacchaṃ akāmayiManusso migiyā saddhiṃ natthi kāme asādiso Handa khohaṃ gamisasāmi sāḷike maṃjubhāṇikePaccakkhānupadaṃ hetaṃ atimaññasi nūna maṃ  Na siri taramānassa māḍhara suvapaṇḍataIdheva tāva acchassu yāva rājānaṃ dakkhasiSossasi saddaṃ mutiṅgānaṃ ānubhāvañca rājino Yo nu khoyaṃ tibbo saddo tirojanapade sutoDhitā pañcālarājassa osadhi viya vaṇṇinīTaṃ dassati videhānaṃ so vivāho bhavissati  Nediso te amittānaṃ vivāho hotu māḍharaYathā pañcālarājassa vedehena bhavissati Banedha  machasaṃ  Sāḷikāyeva  machasaṃ  Yoyaṃ kāme kāmayati  machasaṃ syā Sibbissa  aṭṭhakathā  Sosi  machasaṃ syā Ediso  machasaṃ syā vi  Ānayitvāna vedehaṃ pañcālānaṃ rathesabhoTato naṃ ghātayisasti nāssa sakkhi bhavissati  Handa kho maṃ anujānāhi rattiyo sattamattiyoYāvāhaṃ sivirājassa ārocemi mahosinoLaddho ca me āvasatho sāḷikāya upantikaṃ Handa kho taṃ anujānāmi rattiyo sattamattiyoSace tvaṃ sattarattena nāgacchasi mamantikeMaññe okkantasattaṃ maṃ matāya āgamissasi Tato ca kho so gantvāna māḍharo suvapaṇḍitoMahosadhassa akkhāsi sāḷiyā vacanaṃ idaṃ  Yasseva ghare bhuñejayya bhogaṃTasseva atthaṃ puriso careyya Bhandāhaṃ gacchāmi pure janindaPañcālarājassa puraṃ surammaṃNivesanāni māpetuṃ vedehasasa yasassino Nivesanāni māpetvā vedehasasa yasassinoYadā te pahiṇeyyāmi tadā eyyāsi khattiya  Tato ca pāyāsi pure māhosadhoPañcālarājassa puraṃ surammaṃNivesanāni māpetuṃ vedehasasa yasassino  Nivesanāni māpetvā vedehasasa yasassinoAthassa pahiṇi dutaṃ vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃEhidāni mahārāja māpitaṃ te nivesanaṃ Tato ca rājā pāyāsi senāya caturaṅgiyāAnantavāhanaṃ daṭṭhuṃ phītaṃ kampilliyaṃ puraṃ Tato ca kho so gantvāna brahmadantassa pāhiṇiĀgatosmi mahārāja tava pādāni vandituṃ Dadāhidāni me bhariyaṃ nāriṃ sabbaṅgasobhiniṃSuvaṇṇena paṭicchannaṃ dāsīgaṇapukkhataṃ  Svāgataṃ te vedeha atho te adurāgataṃNakkhattaññeca paripuccha ahaṃ kaññaṃ dadāmi teSuvaṇṇena paṭicchannaṃ dāsīgaṇapukkhataṃ Sāḷikāya  machasaṃ  Tato ca rājā vedeho nakkhantaṃ paripucchathaNakkhantaṃ paripucchitvā brahmadantasasa pāhiṇi Dadāhidāni me bhariyaṃ nāriṃ sabbaṅgasobhiniṃSuvaṇṇena paṭicchannaṃ dāsīgaṇapukkhataṃ Dadāhidāni me bhariyaṃ nāriṃ sabbaṅgasobhiniṃSuvaṇṇena paṭicchannaṃ dāsīgaṇapukkhataṃ Hatthi assā rathā patti senā tiṭṭhanti vammitā Ukkā padintā jhāyanti kinnu maññanti paṇḍitā  Hatthi assā rathā patti senā tiṭṭhanti vammitāUkkā padintā jhāyanti kinnu kāhanti paṇḍitā  Rakkhati taṃ mahārāja cuḷaniyo mahabbaloPaduṭṭho te brahmadatto pāto taṃ ghātayissati  Ubbedhate me hadayaṃ mukhañca parisussatiNibbutiṃ nādhigacchāmi aggidaḍḍhova ātape Kammārānaṃ yathā ukkā anto jhāyati no bahiEvampi hadayaṃ mayhaṃ anto jhāyati no bahi Pamatto mantanātito bhintamantosi khantiyaIdāni kho taṃ tāyantu paṇḍitā mantino janā Akatvāmaccassa vacanaṃ atthakāmahitesinoAntapitirato rāja migo kuṭeva ohito Yathāpi maccho baḷisaṃ maṅkaṃ maṃsena chācitaṃĀmagiddho na jānāti maccho maraṇamattano Evameva tuvaṃ rāja cuḷaneyyassa dhitaraṃKāmagiddho na jānāsi macchova maraṇamattano Sace gacchasi pañcālaṃ khippamattaṃ jahessasi Migaṃ pathānupantaṃva mahantaṃ bhayamessati Vammikā  machasaṃ  Ubbedhati  machasaṃ vi  Khippamatthaṃ  machasaṃ Jahissasi  machasaṃ syā  Patthānu  machasaṃ syā  Bhayamesassi  machasaṃ syā  Anariyarūpo puriso janindaAbhiva ucchaṅgagato isayye Na tena mettiṃ kayirātha dhīroDukkho have kāpurisena saṅgamo  Yantveva jaññā purisaṃ janindaSilavāyaṃ bahusasutoTeneva tettiṃ kayirātha dhīroSukho bhave sappurisena saṅgamo Bālo tuvaṃ phaḷamugosi rājaYo uttamatthāni mayī lapitthoKimevāhaṃ naṅgalakoṭivaddhoAtthāni jānissaṃ yathāpi aññe Imaṃ gale gahetvana nāsetha vijitā mamaYo me ratanalābhassa antarāyāya bhāsati  Mahosadha atitena nānuvijjhanti paṇḍitāKi maṃ assaṃ ca sambaddhaṃ patodeneva vijjhasi Sace passasi mokkhaṃ me khemaṃ vā pana pasasasiTeneva maṃ anusāsa kiṃ atitena vijjhasi Atitaṃ mānusaṃ kammaṃ dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃNa taṃ sakkomi mocetuṃ tvampi jānassu khattiya Santi vehāsayā nāgā iddhimanto yasassinoTepi ādāya gaccheyyuṃ yassa honti tathāvidhā Santi vehāsayā assā iddhimanto yasassinoTepi ādāya gaccheyyuṃ yassa honti tathāvidhā Santi vehāsayā pakkhī iddhimanto yasassinoTepi ādāya gaccheyyuṃ yassa honti tathāvidhā Santi vehāsayā yakkhā iddhimanto yasassinoTepi ādāya gaccheyyuṃ yassa honti tathāvidhā Ḍaṃseyya  machasaṃ syā  Kāpurisehi  machasaṃ  Yadeva  machasaṃ Puriso  machasaṃ  Sambandhaṃ  machasaṃ  Vā  machasaṃ Vehāyasā  machasaṃ syā vehāsasā  vi  Atitaṃ mānusaṃ kammaṃ dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃNa taṃ sakkomi mocetuṃ antalikkhena khattiya  Atiradassi puriso mahante udakaṇṇaveYattha so labhate gādhaṃ tattha so vindate sukhaṃ Evaṃ ambhañca añño ca tvaṃ patiṭṭhā mahosadhaTvaṃ nosi mantinaṃ seṭṭho ambhe dukkhā pamocaya Atitaṃ mānusaṃ kammaṃ dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃNa taṃ sakkomi mocetuṃ tvampi rānassu senaka Suṇohi metaṃ vacanaṃ passasetaṃ mahabbhayaṃSenakaṃdāni pucchāmi kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi  Aggiṃ dvārato dema gaṇhāmase vikatatanaṃ Aññamaññaṃ vadhitvāna khippaṃ hessāma jīvitaṃMā no rājā brahmadatto ciraṃ dukkhena mārayi Suṇohi etaṃ vacanaṃ passasetaṃ mahabbhayaṃPukkusaṃdāni pucchāmi kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi Visaṃ khāditvā miyyāma khippaṃ hessāma jīvitaṃMā no rājā brahamadatto ciraṃ dukkhena mārayi Suṇohi metaṃ vacanaṃ passasetaṃ mahabbhayaṃKāvindaṃdāni pucchāmi kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi Rajjuyā khajjha miyyāma papātā papatemaseMā no rājā buhmadatto ciraṃ dukkhena mārayi Suṇohi etaṃ vacanaṃ passasetaṃ mahabbhayaṃDevindaṃdāni pucchāmi kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi Aggiṃ dvārato dema gaṇhāmase vikatatanaṃ Aññamaññaṃ vadhitvāna khippaṃ hessāma jīvitaṃNa no sakkoti mocetuṃ sukheneva mahosadho  Yathā kadalino sāraṃ anevasaṃ nādhigacchatiEvaṃ anevasamānā naṃ pañahaṃ nājjhagamāmase Mānusakaṃ  vi  Nādhaṃ  machasaṃ  Pajānassu  machasaṃ Vikantanaṃ  machasaṃ syā Rājā  machasaṃ  Yathā simbalino sāraṃ anevasaṃ nādhigacchatiEvaṃ anvesamānāṃ pañhaṃ nājjhagamāmase Adese vata no vutthaṃ kuñajarānaṃva nodakeSakāse dummanussānaṃ bālānamavijānataṃ Ubbedhate me hadayaṃ mukhañca parisussatiNibbutiṃ nādhigacchāmi aggidaḍḍhova ātape Kammārānaṃ yathā ukkā anto jhāyati no bahiEvampi hadayaṃ mayhaṃ anto jhayati no bahi  Tato so paṇḍito dhīro atthadassi mahosadhoVedehaṃ dukkhitaṃ disvā idaṃ vacanamabravi Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabhaAhaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi rāhugahitaṃva candimaṃ Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabhaAhaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi rāhugahitaṃva suriyaṃ Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabhaAhaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi paṅke sattaṃva kuñajaraṃ Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabhaAhaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi peḷābaddhaṃva pantagaṃ Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabhaAhaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi pakkhiṃ baddhaṃva pañajare  Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabhaAhaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi macche jālagateriva Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabhaAhaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi sayoggabalavāhanaṃ Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabhaPañcālaṃ vāhayissāmi kākasenaṃva leḍḍunā Dādu paññā kimatthiyā amacco vāpi tādisoYo taṃ sambādhapakkhannaṃ dukkhā na parimocaye Vuṭṭhaṃ  machasaṃ  Ubbedhati  machasaṃ vi  Rāhuggataṃva  machasaṃRāhuggahitaṃva  syā   Etha māṇavā uṭṭhetha mukha ṃsodhatha sandhino vedeho sahamaccehiummaggena gamissati Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā paṇḍitassānusārinoUmmaggadvāraṃ vivariṃsu yantayutte ca aggaḷe  Purato senako yāti pacchato ca mahosadhoMajjhe ca rājā vedeho amaccaparivārito Ummaggā nikkhamitvāna vedeho nāvamāruhiAbhirūḷhañca taṃ ñatvā anusāsi mahosadho Ahaṃ te sāsuro deva ayaṃ sassu janādhipaYathā mātu paṭipatti evaṃ te hotu sassuyā Yathāpi niyako bhātā saudariyo ekamātukoEvaṃ pañcālacaṇḍo te dayitabbo rathesabha Ayaṃ pañcālacaṇḍi te rājaputti abhijjhitāKāmaṃ karohi te tāya bhariyā te rathesabha  Ārūyha nāvaṃ taramāno kinnu tīrambhi tiṭṭhasiKicchā muttambha dukkhāto yāmadāni mahosadha Nesa dhammo mahārāja yohaṃ senāya nāyakoSenaṅgaṃ parihāpetvā attānaṃ parimocaye Nivesanambhi te deva senaṅgaṃ parihāpitaṃTaṃ dinnaṃ brahmadattena anāyissaṃ rathesabha Appaseno mahāsenaṃ kathaṃ viggayha ṭhassasiDubbalo balavantena vihaññissasi paṇḍita  Appasenopi ce manti mahāsenaṃ amantinaṃJināti rājā rājāno ādiccovudayaṃ tamaṃ Susukhaṃ vata saṃvāso paṇḍitehiti senaka pakkhiva pañajare baddhe macchejālagaterivaAmittahatthatthagate mocayī no mahosadho Umaṅgena  machasaṃ ummaṅgena  syā  Umaṅgā  machasaṃ Sayusuro  sīmu machasaṃ syā  Jānātha  machasaṃ Bandhe  machasaṃ  Evametaṃ mahārāja paṇḍitā hi sukhāvahāPakkhiva pañajare baddhe macche jālagaterivaAmittahatthagate mocayī no mahosadho  Rakkhitvā kasiṇaṃ rattiṃ cuḷaniyo mahabbaloUdentaṃ aruṇuggamahi upakāriṃ upāgami Ārūyha pavaraṃ nāgaṃ balavantaṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃRājā avoca pañcālo cuḷaniyo mahabbalo Sannaddho maṇivammena saramādāya pāṇināPessiye ajjhābhāsittha puthugumbe samāgate Hatthārūhe anikaṭṭhe rathike pattika rakeUpāsanamhi katahatthe vāḷavedhe samāgate Pesetha kuñajare danti balavante saṭṭhihāyaneMaddantu kuñajarā nagaraṃ vedehena sumāpitaṃ Vacchadantamukhā setā tikhiṇaggā aṭṭhīvedhinoPanunnā dhanuvegena sampatantu tirītaraṃ Māṇavā vammino surā citradaṇḍayutāvudhāPakkhandino mahānāgā hatthinaṃ hontu sammukhā Sattiyo teladhotāyo accimantī pabhassarāVijjotamānā tiṭṭhantu sataraṃsā viya tārakā  Āvudhabalavantānaṃ guṇikāyuradhārinaṃEtādisānaṃ yodhānaṃ saṅgāme apalāyinaṃVedeho kuto muccissati sace pakkhiva kāhati Tiṃsa me purisanāvutyo sabbe vekekanicchitā Yesaṃ samaṃ na passāmi kevalaṃ mahimaṃ caraṃ Nāgā ca kappitā danti balavanto saṭṭhibhāyanāYesaṃ khandhesu sobhanti kumārā cārudassanā Pītālaṅkārā pitavasanā pituttaranivāsanāNāgakkhandhesu sobhanti devaputtāva nandane Maddantu machasaṃ Etādisehi  machasaṃ syā vi  Kaḷuṅgeneva  machasaṃ  Vītivattāsu rattisu uggatasmiṃ divākareKiṃsukaṃ phullitaṃ disvā āsacchintā migādhamā Evameva tuvaṃ rāja vedehaṃ parivāriya Āsacchinto gamissasi sigālā kiṃsukaṃ yathā  Imassa hatthapāde ca kaṇṇanāsañca chindathaYo me amittaṃ hatthagataṃ vedehaṃ parimocayi Ima maṃsaṃva pātabbaṃ sule katvā pacantu taṃYo me amittaṃ hatthakataṃ vedehaṃ parimocayi Yathāpi āhabhaṃ cammaṃ pathavyā vitaniyyati Sīhassa atho vyagghassa hoti saṅkusamāhataṃ Evaṃ taṃ vitanitvāna vedhayissāmi sattiyāYo me amittaṃ hatthagataṃ vedehaṃ parimocayi Sace me hatthe ca pāde ca kaṇṇanāsañca checchasiEvaṃ pañcālacaṇḍassa vedeho chedayissati Sace me hatthe ca pāde ca kaṇṇanāsañca checchasiEvaṃ pañcālacaṇḍiyā vedeho chedayissati Sace me hatthe ca pāde ca kaṇṇanāsañca checchasiEvaṃ nandāya deviyā vedeho chedayissati Sace me hatthe ca pāde ca kaṇṇanāsañca checchasiEvaṃ te puttadārassa vedeho chedayissati  Sace maṃsaṃva pātabbaṃ sule katvā pavissasiEvaṃ pañcālacaṇḍassa vedeho chedayissati Sace maṃsaṃva pātabbaṃ sule katvā pavissasiEvaṃ pañcālacaṇḍiyā vedeho chedayissati Sace maṃsaṃva pātabbaṃ sule katvā pavissasiEvaṃ nandāya deviyā vedeho chedayissati Parivāritaṃ  machasaṃ  Siṅgālā  machasaṃ  Imaṃ maṃsañcapātabyaṃ  machasaṃ syā Vihaniyyati  machasaṃ syā  Vibhanitvāna  machasaṃ syā vi Pañcālacandassa  machasaṃ syā  Pañcālacandiyā  machasaṃ syā  Sace maṃsaṃva pātabbaṃ sule katvā pavissasiEvaṃ te puttadārassa vedeho chedayissati Sace maṃ vitanitvāna vedhayissasi sattiyāEvaṃ pañcālacaṇḍassa vedeho chedayissati Sace maṃ vitanitvāna vedhayissasi sattiyāEvaṃ pañcālacaṇḍiyā vedeho chedayissati Sace maṃ vitanitvāna vedhayissasi sattiyāEvaṃ nandāya deviyā vedeho chedayissati Sace maṃ vitanitvāna vedhayissasi sattiyāEvaṃ te puttadārassa vedeho vedhayissatiEvaṃ no mattitaṃ raho vedehena mayā sabha Yathā palasataṃ cammaṃ kontimanti suniṭṭhitaṃUpeti tanutāṇāya sarānaṃ paṭihantave Sukhāvaho dukkhanudo vedehassa yasassinoMatiṃ te paṭibhaññāmi usuṃ palasateniva  Iṅgha passa mahārāja suññaṃ antepuraṃ tavaOrodhā ca kumārā ca tava mātā ca khattiyaUmmaggā nīharitvāna vedehassupanāmitā Iṅgha antepuraṃ mayhaṃ gantvāna vicitātha naṃYathā imassa vacanaṃ saccaṃ vā yadi vā musā Evametaṃ mahārāja yathā āha mahosadhoSuññaṃ antepuraṃ sabbaṃ kākapaṭṭanaka yathā Ito gatā mahārāja nārī sabbaṅgasobhanāKosumbhaphalakasussoṇi haṃsagaggarabhāṇinī Ito nītā mahārāja nārī sabbaṅgasobhanāKosaseyyavasanā sāmā jātarūpasumekhalā Surattapādā kalyāṇi suvaṇṇamaṇimekhalāPārevatakkhi sutanu bimboṭṭhā tanumajjhimā Balasataṃ  machasaṃ  Kontimantā  machasaṃ syā  Balasatenavā  machasaṃ Amaṅgā  machasaṃ ummaṅgā  syā  Sujātā bhujagalaṭṭhiva vellīva tanumajjhimāDīghassā kesā asitā īsakaggapavellitā Sujātā migachāpīva hemantaggisikhārivaNadīva giriduggesu sañchantā khuddaveḷuhi  Nāganāsuru kalyāṇi paṭhamā timbarutthinīNātidīghā nātirassā nālomā nātilomasā Nandāya nūna maraṇena nandasi sirivāhanaAhaññaca nūna nandā ca gacchāma yamasādhanaṃ  Dibbaṃ adhiyase māyaṃ akāsi cakkhumohanaṃYo me amittaṃ hatthagataṃ vedehaṃ parimocayi Adhiyanti mahārāja dibbamāyidha paṇḍitāTe mocayanti attānaṃ paṇḍitā mantino janā Santi māṇavaputta kusalā sandhichedakāYesaṃ katena maggena vedeho mithilaṃ gato  Iṅgha passa mahārāja ummaggaṃ sādhu māpitaṃHatthinaṃ atha assānaṃ rathānaṃ atha patatinaṃĀlokabhūtaṃ tiṭṭhantaṃ ummaggaṃ sādhu niṭṭhitaṃ Lābhā vata videhānaṃ yasasa me edisā paṇḍitāGhare vasanti vijite yathā tvaṃsi mahosadha  Vuttiñca parihārañca diguṇaṃ bhattacetanaṃDadāmi vipulaṃ bhuñja kāme ramassu caMā videhaṃ paccagamā kiṃ videho karissati  Yo cajetha mahārāja bhattāraṃ dhanakāraṇāUbhinnaṃ hoti gārayho attano ca parassa caYāva jiveyya vedeho nāññassa puriso siyā Vediva  machasaṃ syā  Migachāpāva  machasaṃ  Umaṅgaṃ  machasaṃ  Yo cajetha mahārāja bhattāraṃ dhanakāraṇāUbhinnaṃ hoti gārayho attano ca parassa caYāva tiṭṭheyya vedeho nāññassa puriso siyā Dammi nikkhasabhassaṃ te gāmāsitiñca kāsisuDāsisatāni cattāri dammi bhariyāsatañca teSabbaṃ senaṅgamādāya sotthiṃ gaccha mahosadha  Yāvaṃ dadantu hatthinaṃ assānaṃ dviguṇaṃ vidhaṃTappentu antapānena rathike pattikārake Hatthi asse rathe patti gacchevādāya paṇḍitaPassatu taṃ mahārājā vedeho mithilaṃ gataṃ Hatthi assā rathā patti senā padissate mahāCaturaṅgini bhiṃsarūpā kinnu maññanti paṇḍitā Ānando te mahārāja uttamo patidissatiSabbaṃ senaṅgamādāya sotthiṃ patto mahosadho  Yathā petaṃ susānasmiṃ chaḍḍetvā caturo janāEvaṃ kampilliye tyambhā chaḍḍayitvā idhāgatā Atha tvaṃ kena vaṇṇena kena vā pana hetunāKena vā atthajātena attānaṃ parimocayi Atthaṃ atthena vedeha mantaṃ mantenana khattiyaParivārayissaṃ rājānaṃ jambudipaṃva sāgaro Dinnaṃ nikkhasahassaṃ me gāmāsiti ca kāsisuDāsisatāni cattāri dinnaṃ bhariyāsatañca meSabbaṃ senaṅgamādāya sotthinambhi idhāgato  Susukhaṃ vata saṃvāso paṇḍitehīti senakaPakkhiva pañajare baddhe macche jālagaterivaAmittahatthagate movayī no mahosadho  Evametaṃ mahārāja paṇḍitā hi sukhāvahāPakkhiva pañajare baddhe macche jālagaterivaAmittahatthatthagate movayī no mahosadho Āhaññantu sabbavīṇā bheriyo deṇḍimāni caNadantu māgadhā saṅkhā vaggu vadatu dundubhi Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāBahuṃ antaṃ ca pānañca paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ Hatthārūhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakāBahuṃ annañca pānañca paṇḍitassābhihārasuṃ Samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatāBahuṃ antañca pānañca paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ Bahujjano pasannosi disvā paṇḍitamāgatePaṇḍitambhi anuppatte velukkhepo avantathātiMahāummaggakaṇḍaṃ  Sace vo vuyhamānānaṃ sattannaṃ udakaṇṇaveManussabalimesāno nāmaṃ gaṇheyya rakkhasoAnupubbaṃ kathaṃ datvā muñcesi dakarakkhino  Mātaraṃ paṭhamaṃ dajjaṃ bhariyaṃ datvāna bhātaraṃTato sahāyaṃ datvāna pañcamaṃ dajjaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ chaṭṭhāhaṃ dajjamattānaṃ neva dajjaṃmahosadhaṃ Posetā te janetti ca digharattānukampikāChambhi tayi paduṭṭhasmiṃ paṇḍitā atthadassiniAññaṃ upanisaṃ katvā vadhā taṃ parimocayi Taṃ tādisaṃ pāṇadadiṃ orasaṃ gabbhadhāriṇiṃMātaraṃ kena dosena dajjāsi dakarakkhino Māgata saṅkhā  machasaṃ  Nadantu  machasaṃ syā  Dakarakkhasā  machasaṃ syāvi  Padussati  machasaṃ   Daharāviya alaṅkārā dhāreti apiḷandhanaṃDovārike anikaṭṭhe ativelaṃ pajagghati Tatopi paṭirājānaṃ sayaṃ dutāni sāsatiMātaraṃ tena dosena dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino  Itthigumbassa pavarā accantapiyavādini Anuggatā silavati chāyāva anapāyini Akkodhanā paññavati paṇḍitā atthadassiniUbbariṃ kena dosena dajjasi dakarakkhino Khiḍḍhāratisamāpannaṃ anatthavasamāgataṃSā maṃ sakānaṃ puttānaṃ ayācaṃ yācate dhanaṃ Sohaṃ dadāmi sāratto bahuṃ uccāvacaṃ dhanaṃSuduccajaṃ cajitvāna pacchā socāmi dummanoUbbariṃ tena desena dajjāmi dakarakkhino  Yenāvitā jānapadā ānītā ca paṭiggahaṃĀbhataṃ pararajjehi abhiṭṭhāya bahuṃ dhanaṃ Dhanuggahānaṃ pavaraṃ suraṃ tikhiṇamantinaṃBhātaraṃ tena desena dajjāsi dakarakkhino Mayocitā jānapadā ānitā ca paṭiggahaṃĀbhataṃ pararajjehi abhiṭṭhāya bahuṃ dhanaṃ Dhanuggahānaṃ pavaro suro tikhiṇamanti caMayāyaṃ sukhito rājā atimaññati dārako Upaṭṭhānampi me ayye na so eti yathā pureBhātaraṃ tena dosena dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino Saṃjagghati  machasaṃ  Piyabhāṇini  machasaṃ syā  Anupubbatā  machasaṃ syā Uppari  machasaṃ  Dajjāhaṃ  machasaṃ  Ānito  machasaṃ Ābhaṭaṃ  syā  Yenocitā  machasaṃ syā   Ekarattena ubhayo tuvaṃ ca dhanusekhavāUbho jātettha pañcālā pahāyā susamācayā Cariyā taṃ anubandhittho ekadukkhasukho tavaUssukko te divārattiṃ sabbakiccesu vyāvaṭoSahāyaṃ tena dosena dajjāsi dakarakkhino Cariyāya ayaṃ ayye pajagghittho mayā sahaAjjāpi tena vaṇṇena ativelaṃ pajagghati Ubbariyāpi me ayye mantayāmi rahogatoAnāmantā pavisati pubbe appaṭivedito Laddhavāro katokāso ahirikaṃ anādaraṃSahāyaṃ tena dosena dajjahaṃ dakarakkhino Kusalo sabbanimittānaṃ rudaññu āgatāgamoUppāde supine yutto niyyāṇe ca pavesane  Paddho bhummantalikkhasmiṃ nakkhattapadakovidoBrāhmaṇaṃ kena desena dajjāsi dakarakkhino Parisāyampi me ayye milayitvā udikkhatiTasmā ajja bhamuṃ luddaṃ dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino Sasamuddapariyāyaṃ mahiṃ sāgarakuṇḍalaṃVasundharaṃ āvasasi amaccaparivārito Cāturanto mahāraṭṭho vijitāvi mahabbaloPathavyā ekarājāsi yaso te vipulaṃgato Soḷasitthisahassāni āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalāNānājanapadā nariyo devakaññupamā subhā Cariyā maṃ  machasaṃ syā  Sañajagghito  machasaṃ  Saṃjagghati  machasaṃ Upariyāpiha  machasaṃ  Uppāte  machasaṃ  Paṭṭho  machasaṃ syā  Ummilitvā machasaṃ syā  Nāri  machasaṃ syā  Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampannaṃ sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃSukhinānaṃ piyaṃ dīghaṃ jīvitaṃ āhu khattiya Atha tvaṃ kena vaṇṇena kena vā pana hetunāPaṇḍitaṃ anurakkhanto pāṇaṃ cajasi duccajaṃ  Yatopi āgato ayye mama hatthaṃ mahosadhoNābhijānāmi dhirassa anumattampi dukkataṃ Sace ca kismici kāle maraṇaṃ me pure siyāPutte ca me paputte ca sukhāpeyya mahosadho Anāgataṃ paccuppannaṃ sabbamatthaṃ vipassatiAnāparādhakammantaṃ na dajjaṃ dakarakkhino Idaṃ suṇotha pañcālā cuḷaniyassa bhāsitaṃPaṇḍitaṃ anurakkhanto pāṇaṃ cajati duccajaṃ  Mātu bhariyāya bhātucca sakhino brāhmaṇassa caAttano cāpi pañcālo channaṃ cajati jīvitaṃ Evaṃ mahatthikā paññā nipuṇā sādhucintaniDiṭṭhadhamme hitatthāya samparāye sukhāya caDakarakkhasapañho Bheri uppalavaṇṇasi pitā suddhono ahuMātā āsi mahāmāyā amarā bimmasundari Suvo ahosi ānando sāriputtosi cuḷanīMahosadho lokanātho evaṃ dharetha jātakaṃ  Mahā ummaggajātakaṃ navamaṃ  So me putte paputte ca  machasaṃ  Cuḷaneyyassa  machasaṃ Mahiddhikā  machasaṃ mi syā  Diṭṭhadhamma  machasaṃ syā Kevaṭṭo dedattosi talatā cullanandikā pañcālacaṇḍi sunadaridevi cāsi yasassikāAmbaṭṭho āsi kāvindo poṭṭhapādo ca pukkuso piḷotiko ca devindo senakocāpi saccakoDevidumbarā diṭṭhamaṅgalikā sālikācāpi kuṇḍali vedeho lāḷudāyatiImāpi dve gāthāyo bahūsu sihalapotthakesu dissanti syāmapotthake ito visadisā Bheriiccādikā pana deva gāthāyo sabbapotthakesu ekasadisā  Mahāvessantarajātakaṃ  Phusati varavāṇṇahe varassu dasadhā varePathavyā cārupubbaṅgi yaṃ tuyhaṃ manaso piyaṃ  Devarāja namo tyatthu kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayāRammā cāvesi maṃ ṭhānā vātova dharaṇirūhaṃ Na ceva te kataṃ pāpaṃ na ca me tvamasi appiyāPuññañca te parikkhīṇaṃ yena tevaṃ vadāmahaṃ Pantike maraṇaṃ tuyhaṃ vināśāvo bhavissatiPatiggaṇabhāhi me ete vare dasa pacecchato Varaṃ ce me ado sakka sabbabhūtānamissaraSivirājassa bhaddante tattha assaṃ nivesane Nīlanettā nīlabhamu nilakkhi ca yathāmigiPhusati nāma nāmena tatthassaṃ pundadari Puttaṃ labhetha varadaṃ yācayogaṃ amacchariṃPujitaṃ patirājehi kittimantaṃ yasassinaṃ Gabbhaṃ me dhārayantiyā majjhimaṅgaṃ anuttata Kucchi anunnato assa cāpaṃva likhitaṃ samaṃ  Thanā me nappapateyyuṃ palitā nassantu vāsavaKāye rajo na lippetha vajjhaṃ cāpi pamocaye Mayurakoñcābhirude nārivaragaṇāyuteKhujjacelāpakākiṇṇe sutamāgadhavaṇṇite Phussati  machasaṃ syā  Yāvayāgi  maichasaṃ  Anuṇṇataṃ  machasaṃ syā Khujjavelāvakākiṇṇe  syā khujjavelākhakākiṇṇe  vi  Citraggaḷerughusite surāmaṃsappabodhaneSivirājassa bhaddante tattha assaṃ mahesiyā Ye te dasa varā dinnā mayā sabbaṅgasobhaneSivirājassa vijite sabbe te lacchasi vare  Idaṃ vatvāna maghavā devarājā sujampatiPhusatiyā varaṃ datvā anumodittha vāsavo Dasavaragāthā  Tato cutā sā phusati khattiyo upapajjathaJetuntarambhi nagare sañajayena samāgami  Dasa māse dhārayitvāna kāronti purapadakkhiṇaṃVessānaṃ vithisā majjhe janesi phusati mamaṃ Na mayhaṃ mattikaṃ nāmaṃ napi pettikasamabhavaṃJātomhi vessavithiyaṃ tasmā vessantaro ahu  Yadāhaṃ dārako homi jātiyā aṭṭhavassikoTadā nisajja pāsāde dānaṃ dātuṃ vicintayiṃ Bhadayaṃ dadeyyaṃ cakkhumpi maṃsampi rudhirampi caDadeyyaṃ kāyaṃ sāvetvā yadi kovi yācaye mamaṃ Sabhāvaṃ cintayantassa akampitamasaṇṭhitaṃAkampi tattha paṭhavi sineruvanavaṭaṃsakā  Parūḷhakacchanakhalomā paṃkadantā rajassirāPaggayha dakkhiṇaṃ bāhuṃ kiṃ maṃ yāvanti brāhmaṇā Ratanaṃ deva yācāma sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaDadāhi pavaraṃ nāgaṃ īsādantaṃ urūḷhavaṃ Dadāmi na vikampāmi yaṃ maṃ yāvanti brāhmaṇāPabhinnaṃ kañajaraṃ dantiṃ opavuyahaṃ gajuttamaṃ Citraggaḷe ghusite  machasaṃ  Bhaddante  machasaṃ  Phussatiyā  machasaṃ syā vi Yāvako  syā vi maramma potthake na dissanti  Hatthikkhandhato oruyha rājā cāgādhimānasoBrāhmaṇānaṃ adā dānaṃ sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano  Tadāsi yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ tadāsi nigamo sivayo cāpi samāgatāDisvā nāgaṃ niyamānaṃ te rañño paṭivedayuṃ Vidhamaṃ deva te raṭṭhaṃ putto vessantaro tavaKathaṃ no hatthinaṃ dajjā nāgaṃ raṭṭhassa pujitaṃ Kathaṃ no kuñajaraṃ dajjā īsādantaṃ urūḷhavaṃKhettaññuṃ sabbayuddhānaṃ sabbasetaṃ gajuttamaṃ Paṇḍukambalasañachannaṃ pabhīnnaṃ sattumaddanaṃDantiṃ savāḷavijaniṃ setaṃ kelāsasādisaṃ Sasetacchattaṃ savupatheyyaṃ sāthabbaṇaṃ sahatthipaṃAggayānaṃ rājavāhiṃ brāhmaṇanaṃ adā dhanaṃ Sāditaṃ  machasaṃ  Saupādheyyaṃ  machasaṃ supattheyyaṃ  syā Sādhabbanaṃ  machasaṃ  Gajaṃ  machasaṃ imā gāthāyo marammapotthake nadissanti  Annaṃ pānañca so dajja vatthasenāsanāni caEtaṃ kho dānapatirūpaṃ etaṃ kho brāhmaṇārahaṃ Ayaṃ te vaṃsarājā no sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃKathaṃ vessantaro putto gajaṃ hājeti sañjaya Sace tvaṃ na karissasi sivinaṃ vacanaṃ imaṃMaññe taṃ yahaputtena savi hatthe karissare  Kāmaṃ janapado māsi raṭṭhaṃ cāpi vinassatuNāhaṃ sivinaṃ vacanā rājaputtaṃ adūsakaṃPabbājeyyaṃ sakā raṭṭhā putto hi mama oraso Kāmaṃ janapado māsi raṭṭhaṃ cāpi vinassatuNāhaṃ sivinaṃ vacanā rājaputtaṃ adūsakaṃPabbājeyyaṃ sakā raṭṭhā putto hi mama atrajo Nacāhaṃ tassa dubbheyyaṃ ariyasilavato hi soAsilokopi me assa pāpañca pasave bahuṃKathaṃ vessantaraṃ puttaṃ satthenana ghātayāmase Mā taṃ daṇḍena satthena na hi so bandhanāhoPabbājehi ca naṃ raṭṭhā vaṅke vasatu pabbate Eso ce sivinaṃ chando chandaṃ na panudāmaseImaṃ so vasatu rattiṃ kāme ca paribhuñjatu Tato ratyā vivasane suriyassuggamanampati Samaggā sivayo hutvā raṭṭhā pabbājayantu naṃ  Uṭṭhehi katte taramāno gantvā vessantaraṃ vadaSivayo deva te kuddhā negamā ca pabbājayanti taṃ Sabbe  machasaṃ  Tasmiṃ  machasaṃ syā  Suriyuggamate sati  machasaṃ  Sa kantā taramānova sivirājena pesitoĀmuttahatthābharaṇo suvattho candanabhusito Sīsaṃ nahāto udakeso pabbājayanti taṃ Kismiṃ me sivayo kuddhā nāhaṃ passāmi dukkhataṃ Tamme katte viyācikkha kasmā pabbājayanti maṃ  Uggā ca rājaputtā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāHatthāruhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā
