navikampeyyaṃ dane me ramati mano Sakaṃ  machasaṃ  Ramāno  machasaṃ  Suriyuggane sati  machasaṃ Yo na passāmi dukkaṭaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Kāmaṃ maṃ sivayo sabbe pabbājentu hanantu vāNeva dānā viramissaṃ kāmaṃ chindantu sattadhā Evaṃ taṃ sivayo āhu negamā ca samāgatāKontimārāya tirena giraṃ ārañajaraṃ patiYena pabbajitā yanti tena gacchatu subbato  Sohaṃ tena gamissāmi yena gacchanti dusakāRattindivaṃ me khamatha yāva dānaṃ dadāmahaṃ Āmantayittha rājā naṃ maddiṃ sabbaṅgasobhanaṃYaṃ te kiñci mayā dinanaṃ dhanaṃ dhaññaca vijjati Hiraññaṃ vā suvaṇṇaṃ vā muttā veḷuriyā bahuSabbaṃ taṃ nidaheyyāsi yañca te petatikaṃ dhanaṃ Tamabuvi rājaputti maddi sabbaṅgasohanāKuhiṃ deva nidaheyyāmi tamme akkhāhi pucchito Silavantesu dajjāsi dānaṃ maddi yathārahaṃNa hi dānā paraṃ atthi patiṭṭhā sabbapāṇinaṃ  Puttesu maddi dayyāsi sassuyā sasuramhi caYo ca taṃ bhattā maññeyya sakkaccaṃ taṃ apaṭṭhahe No ve taṃ hattā maññeyya mayā vippavasena teAññaṃ bhattāraṃ pariyesa mā kisittha mayā vinā Ahaṃ hi vanaṃ gacchāmi ghoraṃ vāḷamigāyutaṃSaṃsayo jīvitaṃ mayhaṃ ekakassa brahāmane Tamabravi rājaputti maddi sabbaṅgasobhanāAbhumme kathaṃ nu bhaṇasi pāpakaṃ vata bhāsasi Nesa dhammo mahārāja yaṃ tvaṃ gaccheyya ekakoAhampi tena gacchāmi yena gacchasi khattiya Maraṇaṃ vā tayā saddhiṃ jīvitaṃ vā tayā vināTadeva maraṇaṃ seyyo yañce jive tayā vinā Nidahāmi  machasaṃ syā  Dajjesi  machasaṃ syā  Dayesi  machasaṃ syā vi Sasasurā  machasaṃ vi  Ekikassa  machasaṃ  Aggiṃ nijjālayitvāna ekajālasamāhitaṃTattha me maraṇaṃ seyyo yañce jive tayā vinā  Yathā āraññakaṃ nāgaṃ dantiṃ anveti hatthinīJessantaṃ giriduggesu samesu visamesu ca Evaṃ taṃ anugacchāmi putte ādāya pacchatoSubharā te bhavissāmi na te hessāmi dubbharā Ime kumāre pasusanto mañjuke piyabhāṇino Āsine vanagumbasmiṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Ime kumāre pasusanto mañjuke piyabhāṇinoKīḷante vanagumbasmiṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Ime kumāre pasusanto mañjuke piyabhāṇinoAssame ramaṇiyamhi na rajjassa sarissasi Ime kumāre pasusanto mañjuke piyabhāṇino Kīḷanne assame ramma na rajjassa sarissasi Ime kumāre pasusanto maladhāri alaṅkateĀssame ramaṇiyamhi na na rajjassa sarissasi Ime kumāre pasusanto maladhāri alaṅkateKīḷante assame ramme na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā dakkhisi naccante kumāre maladhārino Āssame ramaṇiyamhi na na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā dakkhisi naccante kumāre maladhārinoKīḷante āssame ramaṇiyamhi na na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā dakkhisi mātaṅgaṃ kuñajaraṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃEkaṃ araññe vicarantaṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā dakkhisi mātaṅgaṃ kuñajaraṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃSāyaṃ pāto vicarantaṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Piyābhāṇine  machasaṃ syā  Āsane  machasaṃ  Māladhārine  machasaṃ syā vi Sāraṃ  machasaṃ   Yadā kaṇerusaṅghassa yuthassa purato cajaṃKoñcaṃ kābhati mātaṅgo kuñajaro saṭṭhihāyanoTassa taṃ nadato sutvā na rajjassa sarissasi Dubhato vanavikāse yadā dakkhisi kāmadaṃ Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe na rajjassa sarissasi Migaṃ disvana sāyanhaṃ pañcamālikamāgataṃ Kimpurise ca naccante na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā sossasi nigghosaṃ sandamānāya sindhuyāGitaṃ kimpurisānañca na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā sossisi nigghosaṃ girigabbharacārinoVassamānassa lukassa na rajjassa sarissasasi Yadā sihassa vyagghassa khaggassa gavayassa caVane sosassi vāḷānaṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā morihi parikiṇṇaṃ barihinaṃ matthakāsinaṃMoraṃ dakkhisi naccantaṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā morihi parikiṇṇa aṇḍajaṃ citra pekkhunaṃ Moraṃ dakkhisi naccannaṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā morihi parikiṇṇa nilagīvaṃ sikhaṇḍinaṃMoraṃ dakkhisi naccannaṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā dakkhisi hemante pupphate dharaṇiruheSurabhisampavāyante na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā hemantike māse haritaṃ dakkhisi mediniṃInadagopakasañachannaṃ na rajjassa sarissasi Yadā dakkhisi hemante pupphite dharaṇiruheKuṭajaṃ bimbajālañca pupphitaṃ lomapadamakaṃ Indagopakavaṇṇahā gandārā paṇḍukambalāYāyantamanuyāyanti svājjekova gamissati Yo pubbe hatthinā yāti sivikāya rathena caSvājja vessantaro rājā kathaṃ gacchati pattiko Kathaṃ candanalintaṅgo naccagitappakodhanoKharājinaṃ pharasuñca khārikājañca bhāhiti Kasmā nābhihariyanti kāsāvā ajānāni vāPavisantaṃ buhāraññaṃ kasmā ciraṃ na khajjhare Kathannu ciraṃ dhārenti rājapabbajitā janāKathaṃ kusamayaṃ ciraṃ maddī paridahessati Kāsiyāni ca dhāretvā khomakodumbarāni ca Kusacirāni dhārenti kathaṃ maddi karissati Vayhāhi pariyāyitvā sivikāya rathena caSā kathajja anuccaṅgi pathaṃ gacchati pattikā Yassā mudutalā hatthā caraṇā ca sukhedhitāSā kathajja anuccaṅgi vanaṃ gacchati hirukā Yassā mututalā pādā caraṇā ca sukhedhitā Pādukāhi suvaṇṇāhi piḷamānāma gacchatiSā kathajja anuccaṅgi machasaṃ vi  Yāssu itthi sahassassa purato gacchati māliniSā kathajja anuccaṅgi vanaṃ gacchati ekikā Yāssu sivāya sutvāna muhuṃ anatasate pureSā kathajja anuccaṅgi vanaṃ gacchati hirukā Yāssu indassa gottassa uḷukassa pavassatoSutvāna nadato bhītā vāruṇiva pavedhatiSā kathajja anuccaṅgi vanaṃ gacchati hīrukā Sakuṇi hataputtāva suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃCiraṃ dukkhena jhāyissaṃ suññaṃ āgammimaṃ puraṃ kulāvakaṃCiraṃ dukkhena jhāyissaṃ suññaṃ āgammimaṃ puraṃ Kurarī hatachāpāva suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃKisā paṇḍu bhavissāmi piye putte apassati Kurarī hatachāpāva suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃTena tena ca vesiyānā ca brahmaṇāBāhā paggayha pakkanaduṃ vessantaranivesane Hatthārūhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakāBāhā paggayha vessantaranivesane Tato ratyā vivasane suriyassuggamanaṃ patiAtha vessantaro rājā dānaṃ dātuṃ upāgami Vatthāni vatthakāmānaṃ soṇaḍānaṃ detha vāruṇiṃBhojanaṃ bhojanatthinaṃ sammā detha pacecchatha Mā ca kañci vaṇibbake heṭhayittha idhāgateTappetha annapānena gacchantu paṭipujitā Tesu mantā kiḷantāva sampatanti vaṇibbakāNikkhamanne mahārāje sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhate Acchecchuṃ vata bho rukkhaṃ sabbakāmadadaṃ dumaṃYathā vessantaraṃ raṭṭhā pabbājenti adūsakaṃ Acchecchuṃ ahuNikkhamante mahārāje sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane Ye brāhmaṇā ye ca samaṇā aññevāpi vaṇibbakāBāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ adhammo kira bho iti Yathā vessantaro rājā yajamāno sake pureSivinaṃ vacanatthena datvā sabbālaṅkārabhusiteĀjāniye ca jātiyā sindhave sīghavāhane Arūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi illiyācāpadhārihiEsa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati Santa rathasate datvā santaddhe ussitaddhajeDīpe athopi veyyaghge sabbālaṅkārabhusite Arūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihiEsa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati Satta itthisate datthā ekamekā rathe ṭhitāSannaddhā nikkharajjuhi suvaṇṇena alaṅkatā Pītālaṅkārā pītavasanā pitābharaṇabhusitāĀḷārapakhumā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimāEsa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati Āḷārapambhā  machasaṃ  veyyaghge  veyyagghe  Santa dhenusate datvā sabbā kaṃsupadhāraṇā Esa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati Sattadāsisate datvā sattadāsasatāni caEsa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati Hatthi asse rathe datvā nāriyo ca alaṅkatāEsa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati Tadāsiṃ yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ tadāsi lomahaṃsanāMahādāne padinnamhi medini samakampatha Tadāsiṃ yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ tadāsi lomahaṃsanāYaṃ pañajalikato rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati anappakoEkassa kāraṇā mayhaṃ hiṃseyyuṃ bahuke jane Purakkhitvā  machasaṃ  Paricāritvāna  machasaṃ  Āsuṃ  machasaṃ Balaggā  machasaṃ syā  Bahuko jano  machasaṃ vi  Paṭiggahitaṃ yaṃ dinnaṃ sabbassa nāmenāmittatāpanā Tā naṃ tattha gatāvocuṃ nadīudakahārikā Thiyo naṃ paribhāsiṃsu samāgantvā kutubhalā Amittā nūna te mātā amitto nūna te pitāYe taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ Abhitaṃ vata te ñāti mantayiṃsu rabhogatāYe taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ Dukkaraṃ vata te ñāti mantayiṃsu rabhogatāYe taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ Pāpakaṃ vata te ñāti mantayiṃsu Mamāpaya  machasaṃ Bhāriyā  machasaṃ vi  Abhinaṃ  machasaṃ syā vi  Dukkaṭaṃ  machasaṃ vi   Amanāpavāsaṃ vasasi jiṇṇena patinā sahaYā tvaṃ vasasi jiṇṇassa matante jīvitā maraṃ Na hi nūna tuyhaṃ kalyāṇi pitā mātā ca sobhaneAññaṃ bhattāraṃ vindiṃsu ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsuEvaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ Duyayiṭṭhaṃ te navamiyaṃ akataṃ aggihuttakaṃYe taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ Samaṇe brāhmaṇe nūna brahmacariyaparāyaṇeSā tvaṃ loke abhisapi silavante bahussuteYā tvaṃ vasasi jiṇṇassa evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ Na dukkhaṃ abhinā daṭṭhaṃ na dukkhaṃ sattiyā hataṃTañca dukkhañca tippañca yaṃ passe jiṇṇakaṃ patiṃ Natthi khiḍḍā natthī rati jiṇṇena patinā sahaNatthī allāpasallapo jagghitampi na sohati Yadā ca daharo daharā mantayanti rabhogatāSabbesaṃ sokā nassanti ye keci hadayanissitā Daharā tvaṃ rupavati purisānaṃ abhipatthitāGaccha ñāti kule accha kiṃ jiṇṇo ramayissati  Na te brāhmaṇa gacchāmi nadiṃ adakahāriyāThiyo maṃ paribhāsanti tayā jiṇṇena buhmaṇa Mā me tvaṃ akarā kammaṃ mā me udakamāhariAhaṃ udakamāhissaṃ mā hoti kupitā ahu Nāhaṃ kamhi kule jātā yaṃ tvaṃ udakamāhareEvaṃ brahmaṇa jānāhi na te vacchāmahaṃ ghare Sace me dāsaṃ dāsiṃ vā nānayisassi brāhmaṇaEvaṃ brahmaṇa jānāhi na te vacchāmi santike Tibbañca  machasaṃ  Jagghītumpi  Sabbe sokā vinassanti  syā sabbā sokā  machasaṃ  Natthi me sippaṭaṭhānaṃ vā dhanaṃ dhaññacca brāhmaṇīṃKutohaṃ dāsaṃ dāsiṃ vā ānayissāmi bhotiyāAhaṃ hotiṃ upaṭṭhissaṃ mā hoti kupitā ahu Ehi te abhamakkhissaṃ yathā me vacanaṃ sutaṃ Esa vessantaro rājā vaṅke vasati pabbate Taṃ tvaṃ gantvāna yācassu dāsaṃ dāsiṃ ca brāhmaṇaSo te dassati yācito dāsaṃ dāsiñca khattiyo Jiṇṇohamasami abalo dīgho vaddhā suduggamoMā hoti paridevesi mā ca tvaṃ vimanā ahuAhaṃ bhotiṃ upaṭṭhissaṃ mā bhoti kupitā ahu  Yathā agantvā saṅgāmaṃ ayuddhova parājitoEvameva tuvaṃ brahme agananvā parājito Sace me dāsiṃ vā nānayissasi brāhmaṇaEvaṃ brahmaṇa jānāhi na te vacchāmahaṃ ghareAmanapaṃ te karissāmi taṃ te dukkhaṃ bhavissati Nakkhatte utupabbesu khiyetha datvā nānutapeyyabhaṃDadaṃ cittaṃ pasādeyyaṃ sattametaṃ varaṃ vare  Ito cimuccamānāhaṃ saggagāmī visesaguAnibbatti tato assaṃ aṭṭhametaṃ varaṃ vare Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā devindo etadabraviAciraṃ vata te tāto pitā taṃ diṭṭhumessati Idaṃ vatvāna maghā devarājā sujampatiVessantare varaṃ datvā saggakāyaṃ apakkami Sakkapabbaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ   Kassetaṃ mukhamābhāti hemaṃ vuttattamaggināNikkhaṃva jātarūpassa ukkāmukhapabhaṃsitaṃ Ubho sadisapacacaṅgā ubho sadisalakkhaṇāJālassa dasiso eko ekā kaṇhājinā yathā  Sīhā bilāva nikkhantā ubho sampatirūpakāJātarūpamayā yeva ime dissanti dārakā Kuto nu tvaṃ bhāradvāja ime ānesi dārakeAjja raṭṭhamanuppatto kuto āgacchasi brāhmaṇa Mayhante dārakā deva dinnā vintena yañajayaAjja pantarasā ratti yato dinnāme dārāka  Kena vā vāvapeyyena sammāñāyena saddaheKo te taṃ dānamaddā puttake dānamuttamaṃ Yo yāvataṃ patiṭṭhāsi bhūtānaṃ dharaṇirivaSo me vessantaro rājā puttedāsi vane vasaṃ Yo yāvataṃ gati āsi savanatinaṃva sāgaroSo me vessantaro rājā puttedāsi vane vasaṃ Dukkaṃ vata bho raññā saddhena gharamesināKathaṃ nu puttake dajjā araññe avaruddhako Imaṃ bhonto nisāmetha yācantettha samāgatāKathaṃ me vessantaro rājā puttedāsi vane vasaṃ Dāsaṃ dāsiñca so dajjā assaṃ vāssatarīrathaṃ Hatthiñca kuñajaraṃ dajjā kathaṃ so dajjā dārake Yassa nanthi ghare dāso asso vāssatarirathoHatthi ca kuñajaro nāgo kiṃ so dajjā pitāmabha  Dānamassa pasaṃsāma na ca nindāma puttakāNathannu hadayaṃ āsi tumbhe datvā vaṇibbake Bhavaṃ  machasaṃ  Kuhiṃ gacchasi brāhmaṇa  machasaṃ  Laddhā  syā  Vācāyapoyyena  syā kena vācāpeyyena  machasaṃ  Assaṃ cassatarirathaṃ  machasaṃ Nassa  machasaṃ nāssa  syā  Nāvanindāma  machasaṃ syā  Drakkhassa hadayaṃ āsi atho uṇhampi passasiRohiṇiheva tambakkhi pitā assuni vattayi Yaṃ taṃ kaṇhājināvoca ayaṃ maṃ tāta brāhmaṇoLaṭṭhiyā patikoṭeti ghare jātaṃva dāsiyaṃ Na cāyaṃ brāhmaṇo tāta dhammikā honti brāhmaṇāYakkho brāhmaṇavaṇeṇana kādituṃ tāta neti noNiyamāne pisācena kinnu tātā udikkhasi Rājaputti ca vo mātā rājaputto ca vo pitāPubbe me aṅkamāruyha kinnu tiṭṭhatha ārakā Rājaputti ca vo mātā rājaputto ca vo pitāDāsā mayaṃ brahmaṇassa tasmā tiṭṭhatha ārakā Mā sammecaṃ avavacuttha dayhate hadayaṃ mamaCitakā viya me kāyo āsane na sukhaṃ labhe Mā sammecaṃ avavacuttha bhiyyo sokaṃ janetha maṃNikkhiṇissāmi daṇḍena na vo dāsā bhavissatha  Kimagghiyaṃ hi vo tāta brāhmaṇassa pitā adāYathābhūtaṃ me akkhātha paṭipādentu brāhmaṇaṃ Ahassagghaṃ hi maṃ tāta brāhmaṇassa pitā adāAcchaṃ kaṇhājinaṃ kaññaṃ hatthinā ca satena ca Uṭṭhehi katte taramāno brāhamaṇassa avākara Dāsisataṃ dāsasataṃ gavaṃ hatthusabhaṃ sataṃJātarūpasabhassañca puttānaṃ dehi nikkayaṃ Tato katte taramāno brāhamaṇassa avākariDāsisataṃ dāsasataṃ gavaṃ hatthusabhaṃ sataṃJātarūpasabhassañca puttānaṃ dāsi nikkayaṃ Nikkiṇatvā nāhāpetvā bhojayitvāna dārakeSamalaṅkaritvā bhaṇḍena ucchaṅge upavesayuṃ Citakāyaṃva  machasaṃ  Hatthi ādikena ca  syā hatthinādisatteca  machasaṃ Avākari  machasaṃ   Sīsaṃ nahate sucivatthe sabbābharaṇabhusiteRājā aṅke karitvāna ayyako paripucchatha Kuṇḍale ghusite māle sabbālaṅkārabhusite Rājā aṅke karitvāna idaṃ vacanamabravi Kacci ubo arogā te jāli mātāpitā tavaKacci uñechana yāpenti kacci mulaphalā bahu Kacci ḍaṃsā ca makasā ca appameva siriṃsapāVane vālamigākiṇeṇa hiṃsā tesaṃ na vijjati  Atho ubho aroga me deva mātāpitā mamaAtho uñechana yāpenini atho mulaphalā bahu Ato ḍaṃsā ca makasā ca appameva siriṃsapāVane vālamigākiṇeṇa hiṃsā tesaṃ na vijjati Khaṇantālukamambāni biḷāli takkalāni caKolaṃ bhallāṭakaṃ belalaṃ sā no āhacca posati Yañceva sā āharati vanamulaphalabhārikāTaṃ no sabbe samāgantvā rattiṃ bhañajāma no divā Ammā ca no kisā paṇḍu āharanti dumapphalaṃVātātapena sukhumāli padumaṃ hatthagatāmiva Ammāya patanu kesā vicarantyā brahāvaneVane vālamigākiṇeṇa khaggadipinisevite Kesesu jaṭaṃ banadhitvā kacche jallamadhārayiCammavāsi chamā seti jātavedaṃ namassati Puttā piyā munussānaṃ lokasmiṃ udapajjisuṃNaha nunambhākaṃ ayyassa putte senaho ajāyatha  Dukkatañca hino putta bhunahaccā kataṃ mayāYohaṃ sivinaṃ vacanā pabbājesiṃ adūsakaṃ Sabbābharaṇabhusite  machasaṃ  Kaccibhiṃsā na vijjati  machasaṃ  Dumupaphalaṃ machasaṃ  Yaṃ me kiñci idha dhanaṃ dhaññaca vijjatiEtu vessantaro rājā siviraṭṭhe pasāsatu Na deva mayhaṃ vacanā ehiti sivisuttamoSayameva devo ganatvanā siñca bhogehi atrajaṃ Tato senāpatiṃ rājā sañajayo ajjhabhāsathaHatthi assā rathā patti senā sannāhayantu naṃNegamā ca maṃ anventu brāhmaṇā ca purohitā Tato saṭṭhisahassāni yudhino cārudasasnāKhippamāyantu sannaddhā nānāvaṇeṇahilaṅkatā Nilavatthadharāneke pitāneke nivāsitāAññe lohitauṇhisā suddhāneke nivāsitāKhippamāyantu sannaddhā nānāvatthehilaṅkatā Himāvā yathā gandhadharo pabbato gandhamādanoNānārukkhehi sañachanto mahābhūtagaṇālayo Osadhehi ca dibbehi disā bhāti pavāti caKhippamāyantu sannaddhā nānāvatthehilaṅkatā Tato nāgasabhassāni yojayantu catuddasaSuvaṇaṇakacchā mātaṅgā hemakappanavāsasā Ārūḷā gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihiKhippamāyantu sannaddhā hatthakkhandhehi dassitā Tato assasahassāni yojayantu catuddasaĀjāniyāva jātiyā sindhanā sīghavāhanā Ārūḷā gāmaṇiyehi illiyā cāpadhārihiKhippamāyantu sannaddhā assapiṭṭhahilaṅkatā  Tato rathasahassāni yojayantu catuddasā Ayo sukatanemiyo suvaṇaṇacitapakkhare Nānāvaṇeṇahi  machasaṃ  Disā bhāti pavātiva  machasaṃ  Indiyā  machasaṃ Cātuddasa  machasaṃ  Āpentu dhaje tattha camamāni kavacāni caVipphālentu ca cāpāni daḷahadhammā pahārinoKhippamāyantu sannaddhā rathesu rathajivino Lājā olopiyā pupphā mālāgandhavilepanāAgghiyāni ca tiṭṭhantu yena maggena ehiti Gāme gāme sataṃ kumbhā cubhoBrāhmaṇassa dhanaṃ datvā putta mā bhāyi asasasa Ṇusā  machasaṃ  Jīvitaṃ  machasaṃ  Dame assaṃva  machasaṃ dametyassaṃva syāvi  Jivi  machasaṃ syā vi  Assāsa  machasaṃ  Kaccinnu tāta kusalaṃ kacci tāta anāmayaṃKaccinnu tāta me mātu cakkhuṃ na parihāyati Kusalaṃ ceva me putta atho putta anāmayaṃAthopi putta te mātu cakkhuṃ na paribhāyati Kacci arogaṃ yoggaṃ te kacci vahati vāhanaṃKacci phitā janapadā kacci muṭṭhi na chijjati Atho ārogaṃ yoggaṃ me atho vahati vāhanaṃAtho phitā janapadā atho vuṭṭhi na jijjati  Iccevaṃ mantayantānaṃ mātā nesaṃ adissathaRājaputti giridvāre pattikā anupāhanā Tañca disvāna āyantiṃ mātaraṃ puttagiddhinaṃVessantaro ca maddī ca paccuggantvā avandisuṃ Maddi ca sirasā pāde sassusā abhivādayiMaddi ahambhi te ayye pāde vandāmi te husā  Maddiñca puttakā disvā durato sotthimāgatāKandintā abhidhāviṃsu vacchā bālāva mātaraṃ Maddi ca puttake disvā durato sotthimāgate vāruṇi va pavedhentithanadhārābhisiñcatha  Samātānaṃ ñātinaṃ mahāghoso ajāyathaSabbatā kilesamattanoĀnandi citta sumanā putto saṅgamma lakakhaṇā Idañca paccayaṃ laddhā pubbe kilesamattanoĀnandi citta patitā saha puttehi lakakhaṇā Ekabhattā pure āsiṃ niccaṃ thaṇḍilasāyiniIti metaṃ vataṃ Kappāpasikañca koseyyaṃ khomakodumbarāni caSassu suṇhāya pāhesi yehi madadi asobhatha Tato khomañca kāyuraṃ aṅgadaṃ maṇimekhalaṃSsasu suṇahāya pāhesi yehi maddi asobhatha Tato khomañca kāyuraṃ giveyyaṃ ratanāmayaṃSsasu suṇahāya pāhesi yehi maddi asobhatha Uṇṇathaṃ mukhaphullañca nānāratte ca māṇiye Ssasu suṇahāya pāhesi yehi maddi asobhatha Uggatthanaṃ giṅgamakaṃ mekhalaṃ paṭipādukaṃ Ssasu saṭṭhisahassāni yudhinocārudassanāSamantā parikariṃsu vessantare payātamhi sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāSamantā parikariṃsu vessantare payātamhi sivinaṃ bahupākāratoraṇaṃ Upetaṃ annapānehi naccagitehi cubhayaṃ Vittā jānapādā āsuṃ negamā ca samāgatāAnuppatte kumārambhi sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane Celukhepo avattittha āgate dhanadāyakeNandippavesi nagare
